# Codex Code Review Skill

## Trigger Conditions

Triggered when user input contains:

- "代码审核", "代码审查", "审查代码", "审核代码"
- "review", "code review", "review code", "codex 审核"
- "帮我审核", "检查代码", "审一下", "看看代码"

## Core Concept: Intention vs Implementation

Running `codex review --uncommitted` alone only shows AI "what was done (Implementation)".
Recording intention first tells AI "what you wanted to do (Intention)".

**"Code changes + intention description" as combined input is the most effective way to improve AI code review quality.**

## Skill Architecture

This skill operates in two phases:

1. **Preparation Phase** (current context): Check working directory, update CHANGELOG
2. **Review Phase** (isolated context): Invoke Task tool to execute Lint + codex review (using context: fork to reduce context waste)

## Execution Steps

### 0. [First] Check Working Directory Status

```bash
git diff --name-only && git status --short
```

**Decide review mode based on output:**

- **Has uncommitted changes** → Continue with steps 1-4 (normal flow)
- **Clean working directory** → Directly invoke codex-runner: `codex review --commit HEAD`

### 1. [Mandatory] Check if CHANGELOG is Updated

**Before any review, must check if CHANGELOG.md contains description of current changes.**

```bash
# Check if CHANGELOG.md is in uncommitted changes
git diff --name-only | grep -E "(CHANGELOG|changelog)"
```

**If CHANGELOG is not updated, you must automatically perform the following (don't ask user to do it manually):**

1. **Analyze changes**: Run `git diff --stat` and `git diff` to get complete changes
2. **Auto-generate CHANGELOG entry**: Generate compliant entry based on code changes
3. **Write to CHANGELOG.md**: Use Edit tool to insert entry at top of `[Unreleased]` section
4. **Continue review flow**: Immediately proceed to next steps after CHANGELOG update

**Auto-generated CHANGELOG entry format:**

```markdown
## [Unreleased]

### Added / Changed / Fixed

- Feature description: what problem was solved or what functionality was implemented
- Affected files: main modified files/modules
```

**Example - Auto-generation Flow:**

```
1. Detected CHANGELOG not updated
2. Run git diff --stat, found handlers/responses.go modified (+88 lines)
3. Run git diff to analyze details: added CompactHandler function
4. Auto-generate entry:
   ### Added
   - Added `/v1/responses/compact` endpoint for conversation context compression
   - Supports multi-channel failover and request body size limits
5. Use Edit tool to write to CHANGELOG.md
6. Continue with lint and codex review
```

### 2. [Critical] Stage All New Files

**Before invoking codex review, must add all new files (untracked files) to git staging area, otherwise codex will report P1 error.**

```bash
# Check for new files
git status --short | grep "^??"
```

**If there are new files, automatically execute:**

```bash
# Safely stage all new files (handles empty list and special filenames)
git ls-files --others --exclude-standard -z | while IFS= read -r -d '' f; do git add -- "$f"; done
```

**Explanation:**

- `-z` uses null character to separate filenames, correctly handles filenames with spaces/newlines
- `while IFS= read -r -d ''` reads filenames one by one
- `git add -- "$f"` uses `--` separator, correctly handles filenames starting with `-`
- When no new files exist, loop body doesn't execute, safely skipped
- This won't stage modified files, only handles new files
- codex needs files to be tracked by git for proper review

### 3. Evaluate Task Difficulty and Invoke codex-runner

**Count change scale:**

```bash
# Count number of changed files and lines of code
git diff --stat | tail -1
```

**Difficulty Assessment Criteria:**

**Difficult Tasks** (meets any condition):

- Modified files ≥ 10
- Total code changes (insertions + deletions) ≥ 500 lines
- Single metric: insertions ≥ 300 lines OR deletions ≥ 300 lines
- Involves core architecture/algorithm changes
- Cross-module refactoring
- Config: `model_reasoning_effort=xhigh`, timeout 30 minutes

**Normal Tasks** (other cases):

- Config: `model_reasoning_effort=high`, timeout 10 minutes

**Evaluation Method:**

You MUST parse the `git diff --stat` output correctly to determine difficulty:

```bash
# Get the summary line (last line of git diff --stat)
git diff --stat | tail -1
# Example outputs:
# "20 files changed, 342 insertions(+), 985 deletions(-)"
# "1 file changed, 50 insertions(+)"  # No deletions
# "3 files changed, 120 deletions(-)"  # No insertions
```

**Parsing Rules:**
1. Extract file count from "X file(s) changed" (handle both "1 file" and "N files")
2. Extract insertions from "Y insertion(s)(+)" if present (handle both "1 insertion" and "N insertions"), otherwise 0
3. Extract deletions from "Z deletion(s)(-)" if present (handle both "1 deletion" and "N deletions"), otherwise 0
4. Calculate total changes = insertions + deletions

**Important Edge Cases:**
- Single file: `"1 file changed"` (singular form)
- No insertions: Git omits `"insertions(+)"` entirely → treat as 0
- No deletions: Git omits `"deletions(-)"` entirely → treat as 0
- Pure rename: May show `"0 insertions(+), 0 deletions(-)"` or omit both

**Decision Logic (ANY condition triggers xhigh):**
- IF file_count >= 10 → xhigh
- IF total_changes >= 500 → xhigh
- IF insertions >= 300 → xhigh
- IF deletions >= 300 → xhigh
- ELSE → high

**Example Cases:**
- ✅ "20 files changed, 342 insertions(+), 985 deletions(-)" → xhigh (files=20≥10, total=1327≥500, deletions=985≥300)
- ✅ "5 files changed, 600 insertions(+), 50 deletions(-)" → xhigh (total=650≥500, insertions=600≥300)
- ✅ "12 files changed, 100 insertions(+), 50 deletions(-)" → xhigh (files=12≥10)
- ✅ "1 file changed, 400 deletions(-)" → xhigh (deletions=400≥300)
- ❌ "3 files changed, 150 insertions(+), 80 deletions(-)" → high (all conditions fail)
- ❌ "1 file changed, 50 insertions(+)" → high (no deletions, total=50<500)

**Invoke codex-runner Subtask:**

Use Task tool to invoke codex-runner, passing complete command (including Lint + codex review):

```
Task parameters:
- subagent_type: Bash
- description: "Execute Lint and codex review"
- timeout: 1800000 (30 minutes for difficult tasks) or 600000 (10 minutes for normal tasks)
- prompt: Choose corresponding command based on project type and difficulty

Go project - Difficult task:
  go fmt ./... && go vet ./... && codex review --uncommitted --config model_reasoning_effort=xhigh
  (timeout: 1800000)

Go project - Normal task:
  go fmt ./... && go vet ./... && codex review --uncommitted --config model_reasoning_effort=high
  (timeout: 600000)

Node project - Difficult task:
  npm run lint:fix && codex review --uncommitted --config model_reasoning_effort=xhigh
  (timeout: 1800000)

Node project - Normal task:
  npm run lint:fix && codex review --uncommitted --config model_reasoning_effort=high
  (timeout: 600000)

Python project - Difficult task:
  black . && ruff check --fix . && codex review --uncommitted --config model_reasoning_effort=xhigh
  (timeout: 1800000)

Python project - Normal task:
  black . && ruff check --fix . && codex review --uncommitted --config model_reasoning_effort=high
  (timeout: 600000)

Clean working directory:
  codex review --commit HEAD --config model_reasoning_effort=high
  (timeout: 600000)

## User preferences

- when composing the `turnkey-sdk-csharp` `/goal`, the visible constraint was "create the repository under `KyuzanInc`, private, and do not update the current `peak` repository" -> keep standalone repo work isolated from `peak` unless the user explicitly asks for a cross-repo change [Task 1]

## Reusable knowledge

- The early repo-bootstrap pattern used upstream package snapshots and generated lock/docs artifacts rather than hand-porting from memory: `Directory.Packages.props`, `global.json`, `README.md`, `turnkey-sdk-csharp.sln`, `src/Turnkey.Sdk/Turnkey.Sdk.csproj`, `tests/Turnkey.Sdk.Tests/Turnkey.Sdk.Tests.csproj`, `tests/packages.lock.json`, and snapshot trees such as `snapshots/turnkey-http-3.16.0/...` were all part of the visible scaffold [Task 1]
- The target quality bar was strict functional alignment with the original Turnkey Node.js / TypeScript package logic, with `turnkey-sdk-unity` and upstream snapshots used as mapping/reference material rather than as the final authority [Task 1][Task 2]
- The first high-value parity surface was `Encoding.cs`: preserve Unity-specific helpers only where needed, but explicitly port behavior for helpers equivalent to base64, `pointEncode`, `hexToAscii`, `normalizePadding`, and `bs58Check encode`, backed by upstream test vectors and parity tests [Task 2]

## Failures and how to do differently

- Symptom: the new C# port "works" for common cases but diverges from upstream on edge cases. Cause: direct C# rewrites missed TypeScript semantics in length handling, malformed/odd hex parsing, and base64url invalid-character handling. Fix: add upstream-style fixtures first, then patch `Encoding.cs` until parity tests pass [Task 2]
- Symptom: the agent drifts into modifying `peak` while preparing the new repo. Cause: the plan file lived in `peak`, but the deliverable was a separate repository. Fix: keep `peak` as planning/reference context only and do implementation work inside `turnkey-sdk-csharp` [Task 1]

     1	# KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk
     2	
     3	> **Unofficial / community-maintained Turnkey SDK for .NET by Kyuzan Inc.
     4	> Not affiliated with Turnkey, Inc.**
     5	
     6	A NuGet package that lets .NET applications produce signed Turnkey API
     7	requests and decrypt Turnkey credential / export bundles.
     8	
     9	The crypto logic is a 1:1 logical port of the Turnkey TypeScript SDK packages
    10	at the exact versions consumed by the Kyuzan **peak** monorepo:
    11	
    12	| Source npm package         | Version |
    13	|----------------------------|---------|
    14	| `@turnkey/crypto`          | 2.8.8   |
    15	| `@turnkey/http`            | 3.16.0  |
    16	| `@turnkey/api-key-stamper` | 0.5.0   |
    17	| `@turnkey/encoding`        | 0.6.0   |
    18	
    19	The 1:1 logical equivalence is confirmed by multi-round Codex review.
    20	Evidence is committed to [`codex-crypto-reviews/`](./codex-crypto-reviews/).
    21	
    22	For the authoritative Turnkey SDK in TypeScript, see
    23	[`github.com/tkhq/sdk`](https://github.com/tkhq/sdk).
    24	
    25	## Status
    26	
    27	Pre-release, internal-only. Not published to nuget.org. Not for public
    28	production use. Trademark and distribution review pending.
    29	
    30	## Features (planned for v0.1.0)
    31	
    32	- `Turnkey.Encoding` — hex / base58 / base58check / UTF-8 utilities.
    33	- `Turnkey.Crypto` — P-256 key pair generation, HPKE encrypt / decrypt,
    34	  HKDF, Tonelli-Shanks modular square root, Turnkey credential-bundle
    35	  decrypt, Turnkey export-bundle decrypt, Turnkey session JWT signature
    36	  verification.
    37	- `Turnkey.ApiKeyStamper` — ECDSA P-256 stamp for the Turnkey API
    38	  `X-Stamp` header.
    39	- `Turnkey.Http` — typed signed-request builders for the Turnkey API
    40	  activity endpoints used by the peak wallet flow.
    41	
    42	## Target frameworks
    43	
    44	`netstandard2.1` and `net8.0`. Tested on .NET 8.
    45	
    46	## Dependencies
    47	
    48	- `BouncyCastle.Cryptography 2.5.0` — for ECDSA / ECDH / AES-GCM /
    49	  SHA-256 / HMAC / BigInteger / EC point primitives only. **No
    50	  BouncyCastle HPKE / HKDF / KDF wrappers are used.** HPKE, HKDF,
    51	  Tonelli-Shanks, and bundle parsing are direct ports of the upstream
    52	  Turnkey TypeScript logic.
    53	- `System.Text.Json 8.0.5` — source-generated context only
    54	  (`TurnkeyJsonContext`). No reflection-based serialization,
    55	  no `System.Reflection.Emit`. Compatible with IL2CPP AOT trim.
    56	
    57	## Project structure
    58	
    59	```
    60	src/        — production code
    61	tests/      — xunit tests + golden fixtures from pinned Node packages
    62	docs/security/threat-model.md — scope: key handling, signing, crypto
    63	                                primitives, serialization, test-secret handling
    64	codex-crypto-reviews/          — pinned upstream snapshots, source-pin docs,
    65	                                 multi-round Codex review evidence
    66	```
    67	
    68	## Build and test
    69	
    70	```bash
    71	dotnet restore --use-lock-file
    72	dotnet build turnkey-sdk-csharp.sln -c Release
    73	dotnet test  turnkey-sdk-csharp.sln -c Release \
    74	  --collect:"XPlat Code Coverage"
    75	```
    76	
    77	## Contributing
    78	
    79	This repository is private. Contribution policy will be set after v0.1.0.
    80	
    81	## Verification posture
    82	
    83	The equivalence between this C# port and the pinned upstream TypeScript
    84	packages is enforced by four cooperating mechanisms ([plan](./plans/PLAN-EQUIVALENCE-VERIFICATION.md)
    85	Section 5, "Verification strategy — 4 Tier"):
    86	
    87	| Tier | Source of truth | Asserted in C# by |
    88	|---|---|---|
    89	| 1 | Hand-transcribed upstream `__tests__/` values + cross-language hex constants borrowed from `tkhq/sdk` / `swift-sdk` / `dart-sdk` | `tests/EncodingTests.cs`, `tests/CryptoTests.cs`, `tests/ApiKeyStamperTests.cs`, `tests/Fixtures/{encoding,crypto,api-key-stamper}/*.json` |
    90	| 2 | Bytes produced by running the **pinned** upstream npm packages under `tests/Fixtures/Generators/` (Node 20.x, npm overrides `@noble/curves@1.3.0`) | `tests/ApiKeyStamperTests.NodeFixture_StamperByteParity_PureJsRfc6979` |
    91	| 3 | RFC / NIST / SEC2 / BIP standard vectors for each cryptographic primitive (HKDF RFC 5869, etc.) — primitive-level independent oracle of correctness | `tests/CryptoTests.cs` HKDF tests (RFC 5869 A.1–A.3). Other primitive vectors are planned per the equivalence plan but not yet committed; see plan PR-8/PR-9. |
    92	| 4 | Live Turnkey backend — opt-in only via `TURNKEY_TEST_ORG_API_KEY` env var | (out of CI; manual run only) |
    93	
    94	### Coverage matrix
    95	
    96	[`codex-crypto-reviews/coverage-map.sh --check`](./codex-crypto-reviews/coverage-map.sh)
    97	walks every `test()` block in the pinned upstream `__tests__/*.ts` files
    98	and confirms each one either maps to a C# `[Fact]`/`[Theory]` via a
    99	`/// upstream: <relpath>:<line>` annotation or is recorded in
   100	[`coverage-map.na.tsv`](./codex-crypto-reviews/coverage-map.na.tsv) with a
   101	non-empty `N/A` reason. The gate runs in CI and fails the build if a
   102	new upstream test is added without either a C# counterpart or an
   103	explicit N/A reason. See
   104	[`codex-crypto-reviews/coverage-map.md`](./codex-crypto-reviews/coverage-map.md)
   105	for the current matrix.
   106	
   107	### Upstream drift
   108	
   109	[`/.github/workflows/upstream-drift.yml`](./.github/workflows/upstream-drift.yml)
   110	re-hashes every upstream `__tests__/*.ts` and `__fixtures__/*` file at
   111	the pinned git tag SHA once a month. Drift surfaces as a single open
   112	issue per package labelled `upstream-drift`; the workflow updates an
   113	existing issue rather than opening a new one (idempotent). It is NOT a
   114	main-branch CI gate, so it can never block a PR.
   115	
   116	### Uncertainty checklist (read before depending on this SDK in production)
   117	
   118	- [ ] Upstream P-256 ECDSA on `nodecrypto.ts` and `webcrypto.ts`
   119	      runtimes is non-deterministic. The C# port covers **only** the
   120	      `purejs` runtime path (RFC 6979 deterministic-k, low-S), as
   121	      documented in
   122	      [`codex-crypto-reviews/ApiKeyStamper.cs-codex-findings-reconciliation.md`](./codex-crypto-reviews/ApiKeyStamper.cs-codex-findings-reconciliation.md)
   123	      E1/E2.
   124	- [ ] Upstream `@noble/curves` does NOT enforce low-S by default in
   125	      any 1.x version (verified in PR-4 preflight). The C# port DOES
   126	      enforce low-S, which is the standard wire format. Both signatures
   127	      verify against the same public key. The fixture at
   128	      `tests/Fixtures/api-key-stamper/turnkey-stamper-node-vectors.json`
   129	      records the upstream high-S DER bytes AND the C# low-S
   130	      equivalent; both are confirmed to be cryptographic equivalents
   131	      (same r, s_lowS = n - s_highS).
   132	- [ ] Whether SDK HPKE (`@turnkey/crypto.hpkeEncrypt`) is byte-equal
   133	      to RFC 9180 base mode is an open evaluation deferred to plan
   134	      PR-7a. The C# port is wire-compatible with the SDK's bytes for
   135	      decrypt round-trip; full RFC 9180 byte vectors are NOT imported
   136	      until PR-7a confirms equality.
   137	- [ ] APIs deliberately **not ported**: `hpkeAuthEncrypt`,
   138	      `quorumKeyEncrypt`, `extractPrivateKeyFromPKCS8Bytes`,
   139	      `fromDerSignature`, `toDerSignature`, `verifyStampSignature`,
   140	      `verifyRequestStamp`, `encryptOauth2ClientSecret`,
   141	      `encryptOnRampSecret`, `proof.ts`. Justification + peak monorepo
   142	      grep evidence in
   143	      [`codex-crypto-reviews/peak-usage-grep-evidence.md`](./codex-crypto-reviews/peak-usage-grep-evidence.md)
   144	      and the per-file Codex review under
   145	      [`codex-crypto-reviews/`](./codex-crypto-reviews/).
   146	- [ ] Live Turnkey backend e2e is opt-in only (`TURNKEY_TEST_ORG_API_KEY`).
   147	      The CI does not run it, and the SDK is NOT a substitute for an
   148	      end-to-end test against the backend.
   149	- [ ] Cross-language hex constants (`mockSenderPrivateKey`,
   150	      `mockCredentialBundle`, the BIP-39 mnemonic, etc.) used in
   151	      `CryptoTests.cs` are copied verbatim from `tkhq/sdk` at the
   152	      pinned git tag and from `tkhq/swift-sdk` / `tkhq/dart-sdk` for
   153	      cross-implementation triangulation. Their source URLs are in the
   154	      Codex review files.
   155	
   156	## License
   157	
   158	MIT — see [LICENSE](./LICENSE). Upstream Turnkey TypeScript attribution
   159	is recorded in [NOTICE](./NOTICE).

     1	# PLAN: Turnkey C# SDK ↔ 公式実装 同等性検証プラン (v3)
     2	
     3	**Status**: Draft v3 — awaiting Codex plan review (target: review-clean).
     4	
     5	## v3 changes vs v2 (Codex r1 後の修正)
     6	
     7	| Codex r1 指摘 | v3 の修正 |
     8	|---|---|
     9	| `tests/Fixtures/*.json` の link が壊れている (B-行 broken link) | 全箇所を `tests/Fixtures/{encoding,crypto,api-key-stamper}/*.json` に修正 |
    10	| **HPKE/QOS 混同 (致命)**: v2 は「Turnkey HPKE は RFC 9180 でない独自構成」と書いたが、実は SDK `hpkeEncrypt/hpkeDecrypt` ([crypto.ts:88-138](../codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/turnkey-crypto-2.8.8/ts-source/crypto.ts)) は **JSdoc で RFC 9180 を明示**しており構成も HPKE 風。QOS `quorumKeyEncrypt` ([crypto.ts:219+](../codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/turnkey-crypto-2.8.8/ts-source/crypto.ts)) は別物で C# **未ポート** | **canonical wording を Section 2 に統一**: (a) C# が port しているのは SDK HPKE (RFC 9180 を意図) のみ、(b) QOS は scope 外、(c) SDK HPKE が RFC 9180 と byte-equal かは別 PR で評価する step を新設 (PR-7a)。Tier-3 RFC 9180 取り込みは **PR-7a の評価結果次第** で確定する条件付き |
    11	| Tier-2 の決定論性が崩れる: SDK HPKE は ephemeral key 生成、QOS も nonce 生成 → encrypt 出力 bytes は毎回違う | **encrypt の byte snapshot は撤回**。代わりに (a) **SDK 生成済みの round-trip 等価** (上流 Node で encrypt した output を **fixture として固定**しておき、C# で **decrypt して plaintext 等価**を確認)、(b) encrypt 出力構造 (lengths, header bytes) の構造的 assertion、(c) HPKE が ephemeral key を **外部 inject できる private API** が無いか追加調査 (調査結果次第で encrypt の byte snapshot を限定的に復活) |
    12	| @noble/curves v1.3.0 low-S deterministic が load-bearing だが pinned snapshot だけでは証明できない | PR-4 で **transitive deps を exact lock** し、**generator 起動時に既知 vector で `purejs.sign(message, privateKey)` を assert** する pre-flight test を追加。失敗したら fixture 生成中断 |
    13	| monthly drift workflow が unbounded で月毎に issue 量産 | **idempotency rule** を Section 6.4 に追加: `gh issue list --label upstream-drift --json number --jq '.[0].number'` で既存 open issue を 1 つ取得、あれば update、無ければ create。Workflow yaml 例も入れる |
    14	| PR-4 が `tests/turnkey-sdk-csharp.Tests.csproj` の Generators 排除を含んでいない | PR-4 内容に「`<None Remove="Fixtures/Generators/**" />` と `<Content Remove="Fixtures/Generators/**" />` を csproj に追加」を明記 |
    15	| PR-3 規模が plan の表現より大きい | Section 6.1 に **欠落候補テスト名の concrete list** を追加 (Codex r1 列挙分を全部書き出す) |
    16	| Tier-3 で Ed25519 / secp256k1 / Base58Check Bitcoin を忘れている | Section 6.3 に Ed25519 RFC 8032、secp256k1 SEC2、Base58Check Bitcoin double-SHA256 を追加 |
    17	| PR-11 fixture-only seeding は consumer 無し golden data | PR-11 で **`ProofFixtureProvenanceTests` を必ず一緒に追加**: JSON parse、`_provenance` schema 検証、上流 sha256 一致、を assert。verify 実装本体は scope 外を維持 |
    18	| Phase E は `PR-12 (docs)` 誤記 (PR-12 は drift CI) | `PR-14 (docs)` に修正、PR-14 の依存に PR-12/PR-13 を追加 |
    19	| HPKE 説明が Section 2/6.3/10/12 で重複 | Section 2 を canonical source とし、他 3 箇所は `(Section 2 参照)` リンクに置換 |
    20	| "README CI で更新" / "backend accepts means correct" が測定不能 | "README updated and committed in PR-14" / "wire-format byte-equal in Tier-2 fixtures" に置換 |
    21	| 「公式他言語 SDK の test fixture」未検証 (G の unresolved) | Phase A の作業に **`peak/` リポジトリの grep で proof 呼出し有無を確認**する step を明示。他言語 SDK fixture は本プラン scope 外として明記 |
    22	
    23	## v2 changes vs v1 (調査後の修正、参考)
    24	
    25	| v1 の誤り | v2 の修正 |
    26	|---|---|
    27	| 「Tier 3 で HPKE RFC 9180 vectors を取り込む」 | (v3 で再修正) v2 では「Turnkey HPKE は RFC 9180 でない独自方式」とした上で RFC 9180 vectors を撤回したが、これも誤り。v3 で再評価 |
    28	| proof.ts は scope 外で確定 | proof-tests.ts に**実 enclave 由来の `v1AppProof` / `v1BootProof` JSON ゴールデン**があり、cross-language 借用に最適。**proof ポート要否は別計画**を維持しつつ、本プランで `tests/Fixtures/proofs/` を Tier-1 として置く準備 (verify 実装は別計画) を含める |
    29	| 「他言語 SDK に cross-language vector があるかもしれない」 | 公式 cross-language fixture セットは**存在しない**。代わりに `mockSenderPrivateKey=67ee05fc…` 等のハードコード値が `tkhq/sdk` / `swift-sdk` / `dart-sdk` で**完全一致でコピー**。実質的 reference vector として **Tier-1 で借用** |
    30	| Tier-4 (live) | 維持。live e2e は `tkhq/python-sdk` のみが CI に組み込んでおり、他 SDK は mock 中心 |
    31	
    32	## 1. Intent
    33	
    34	`KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk` が **Turnkey 公式 TypeScript SDK
    35	(@turnkey/{crypto,http,api-key-stamper,encoding} の peak-pinned 版)
    36	と機能的に等価** であることを、後付け的なレビューではなく
    37	**機械検証可能な公式由来テストアセット** で恒常的に担保する。
    38	
    39	本プランは、既存の Codex 3-round 行ごと等価レビュー
    40	(`codex-crypto-reviews/`) と既存の Tier-1 fixture
    41	(`tests/Fixtures/{encoding,crypto,api-key-stamper}/*.json`) を
    42	**置き換えるものではない**。
    43	それらが「**人が読んで一致を確認した**」レベルの保証であるのに対し、
    44	本プランは「**入力に対する観測可能な出力を機械で照合し、
    45	上流が変わったら自動で気付く**」レベルの保証を上乗せする。
    46	
    47	「観測可能な出力」は具体的には以下のいずれか:
    48	
    49	- 決定論経路: 入力が同じなら byte 等価 (例: stamp の DER 署名は
    50	  `purejs` runtime で RFC 6979 deterministic-k、credential-bundle decrypt は
    51	  入力 ciphertext + receiver private key で plaintext が一意)。
    52	- 非決定論経路: ephemeral key/nonce を生成するため byte 等価は取れない
    53	  ものに対しては (a) decrypt round-trip での plaintext 等価、
    54	  (b) 構造的 assertion (フィールド長、ヘッダ、JSON キー順、署名検証成功)。
    55	
    56	## 2. Goals (must-have)
    57	
    58	1. **Coverage matrix**: 公式 `__tests__/*.ts` の各 `test()` ブロックが
    59	   C# のどの `[Fact]` / `[Theory]` メソッドに対応するかを 1:1 で
    60	   ドキュメント化する。欠落は CI で fail する。
    61	2. **Byte-equal fixtures**: 公式 npm パッケージを `npm install` した
    62	   Node 環境で生成した実バイト (stamp, signed-request body,
    63	   credential-bundle decrypt 等) を `tests/Fixtures/**` に固定し、
    64	   C# が同一入力で同一バイトを生成することを assert する。
    65	3. **Standard test vectors (primitives + 条件付きで HPKE)**:
    66	   HKDF (RFC 5869)、ECDSA P-256 deterministic-k (RFC 6979)、
    67	   AES-GCM-256 (NIST CAVP)、SHA-256 (NIST SHS)、HMAC-SHA256 (RFC 4231)、
    68	   Ed25519 (RFC 8032、SOLANA export 用) の **個別 primitive** で C# 実装を検証する。
    69	   secp256k1 SEC2 / Base58Check Bitcoin double-SHA256 もここに含める。
    70	   **HPKE 全体 (RFC 9180) の取り込みは条件付き**:
    71	   PR-7a で 「pinned `@turnkey/crypto@2.8.8` の `hpkeEncrypt` が
    72	   RFC 9180 base mode (DHKEM(P-256,HKDF-SHA256) + HKDF-SHA256 + AES-256-GCM)
    73	   と byte-equal か」を `__tests__/crypto-test.ts` の HPKE 経路を
    74	   実 Node で動かして固定 ephemeral key を inject (もし可能なら) し評価する。
    75	   評価結果が **byte-equal なら RFC 9180 Appendix A vectors を取り込み**、
    76	   **byte-equal でなければ取り込まない** (Tier-2 で SDK 生成 bytes を信頼)。
    77	   ※ JSdoc は RFC 9180 を明示するが ([crypto.ts:88-91](../codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/turnkey-crypto-2.8.8/ts-source/crypto.ts))、
    78	   実装の suite_id/labels と RFC 9180 base mode の literal が**完全一致するかは未確認**。
    79	   QOS `quorumKeyEncrypt` は C# **未ポート**であり本プラン scope 外
    80	   (Section 2 canonical 説明を参照)。
    81	4. **Drift detection**: 公式 `__tests__/` の sha256 を pin し、
    82	   月次 cron で再取得して差分があれば **upstream-drift というラベルの
    83	   single open issue を idempotent に update/create する**
    84	   (Section 6.4 / Section 8 / Section 9 で一貫した定義)。
    85	   この workflow は **main CI gate ではない** (= PR をブロックしない)。
    86	   issue が立ったら人手で再 pin と対応 C# テスト更新の PR を立てる。
    87	5. **不確定要素の明示** (PR-14 README "Verification posture" 章で
    88	   以下のチェックリストを必ず文書化する):
    89	   - [ ] 公式 P-256 ECDSA は `nodecrypto.ts` / `webcrypto.ts` ランタイムでは
    90	     non-deterministic。C# 側は **`purejs` ランタイム相当 (RFC 6979 + low-S) のみ
    91	     ports** している事実
    92	     (既に `ApiKeyStamper.cs-codex-findings-reconciliation.md` E1/E2 で合意済み)。
    93	   - [ ] SDK HPKE と RFC 9180 base mode の byte-equality は **PR-7a の判定結果**を
    94	     review posture に明記 (byte-equal / non-equal / inconclusive)。
    95	   - [ ] **未ポート API リスト** (`src/Crypto.cs:25-30` の "Out of scope" コメントと一致):
    96	     `hpkeAuthEncrypt`, `quorumKeyEncrypt`, `extractPrivateKeyFromPKCS8Bytes`,
    97	     `fromDerSignature`, `toDerSignature`, `verifyStampSignature`,
    98	     `verifyRequestStamp`, `encryptWalletToBundle`, `encryptToEnclave`,
    99	     `encryptOauth2ClientSecret`, `encryptOnRampSecret`, `proof.ts`。
   100	   - [ ] live e2e backend 経路は opt-in (`TURNKEY_TEST_ORG_API_KEY` 環境変数) のみ。
   101	   - [ ] cross-language 借用値 (`mockSenderPrivateKey`, `mockCredentialBundle`, etc.)
   102	     の上流 git revision pin。
   103	
   104	### Non-goals
   105	
   106	- 既存の `codex-crypto-reviews/` SOP の置き換え (補強のみ)。
   107	- nuget.org への公開条件の変更。
   108	- 新規機能 (proof.ts 完全移植、QOS `quorumKeyEncrypt` ポートなど) の追加。
   109	  **proof モジュールに対するポート方針は本プランの第 12 章「未スコープ依存」で別計画とする。**
   110	- 公式 Backend に対する live e2e の必須化 (live 経路は opt-in のまま)。
   111	
   112	### 2.1. 暗号構成の canonical 用語 (重要)
   113	
   114	以下の用語は本プラン全体で **canonical** にこの定義で使う。他章 (3, 4, 6.3, 9, 10, 12) は
   115	**この章を再記述せず参照する**。
   116	
   117	- **SDK HPKE**: pinned `@turnkey/crypto@2.8.8` の `hpkeEncrypt` / `hpkeDecrypt` /
   118	  `hpkeAuthEncrypt` 経路。([crypto.ts:88-203](../codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/turnkey-crypto-2.8.8/ts-source/crypto.ts))
   119	  - JSdoc が RFC 9180 を明示。
   120	  - `SUITE_ID_1 = "KEM\0\x10"` (DHKEM(P-256, HKDF-SHA256))、
   121	    `SUITE_ID_2 = "HPKE\0\x10\0\x01\0\x02"` (kem_id=0x0010, kdf_id=0x0001, aead_id=0x0002)
   122	    の literal を使う ([Crypto.cs:77-79](../src/Crypto.cs))。
   123	  - これらの suite_id literal は **RFC 9180 base mode の値と一致**:
   124	    `kem_id=0x0010 = DHKEM(P-256, HKDF-SHA256)`,
   125	    `kdf_id=0x0001 = HKDF-SHA256`, `aead_id=0x0002 = AES-256-GCM`。
   126	    `extractAndExpand(..., 32)` で 32-byte AES key、`extractAndExpand(..., 12)` で
   127	    12-byte IV を派生するのも AES-256-GCM の使用と整合。
   128	  - ただし上記 suite_id 一致は「実装が RFC 9180 と完全互換」を即座に意味しない。
   129	    HPKE label の literal バイト列 (`HPKE-v1`, `eae_prk`, `secret`, `shared_secret`)
   130	    も RFC 9180 と完全一致するかは PR-7a で確認する。
   131	  - **C# `Turnkey.Crypto.HpkeEncrypt` / `HpkeDecrypt` がポートしているのはこの経路のみ**。
   132	    ([Crypto.cs:404-456](../src/Crypto.cs))。
   133	- **QOS encryption**: 同じファイルの `quorumKeyEncrypt` ([crypto.ts:219+](../codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/turnkey-crypto-2.8.8/ts-source/crypto.ts))。
   134	  - jsdoc に「Algorithm originally implemented in qos」と明示。
   135	  - `QOS_ENCRYPTION_HMAC_MESSAGE = "qos_encryption_hmac_message"`、
   136	    SHA-512 HMAC + AES-GCM-256、borsh serialization。
   137	  - **C# **未ポート**。本プラン scope 外**。
   138	- **RFC 9180**: IETF Hybrid Public Key Encryption 仕様。SDK HPKE と完全一致するかは
   139	  PR-7a で評価する別タスク。「SDK HPKE = RFC 9180 と等価」とは現時点で言わない。
   140	
   141	### 2.2. C# が ports している upstream 経路の一覧 (Non-Goal 確認用)
   142	
   143	| C# public API | upstream 関数 | upstream 経路 | C# port 状況 |
   144	|---|---|---|---|
   145	| `Turnkey.Crypto.HpkeEncrypt` | `hpkeEncrypt` | SDK HPKE (RFC 9180 を意図) | **済** |
   146	| `Turnkey.Crypto.HpkeDecrypt` | `hpkeDecrypt` | SDK HPKE | **済** |
   147	| `Turnkey.Crypto.DecryptCredentialBundle` | `decryptCredentialBundle` | SDK HPKE + base58check + AES-GCM | **済** |
   148	| `Turnkey.Crypto.DecryptExportBundle` | `decryptExportBundle` | SDK HPKE + mnemonic/PKCS#8 | **済** |
   149	| `Turnkey.Crypto.EncryptPrivateKeyToBundle` | `encryptPrivateKeyToBundle` | SDK HPKE + base58check | **済** |
   150	| (なし) | `quorumKeyEncrypt` (QOS) | QOS 独自 | **未ポート (scope 外)** |
   151	| (なし) | `verify` / `verifyAppProofSignature` (proof) | P-256/P-384 + COSE/X.509 | **未ポート (proof scope 外)** |
   152	
   153	## 3. 現状アセスメント (Where we are)
   154	
   155	| 項目 | 既存状態 | 備考 |
   156	|---|---|---|
   157	| Upstream pinned snapshots | 4 パッケージ (`crypto@2.8.8`, `http@3.16.0`, `api-key-stamper@0.5.0`, `encoding@0.6.0`) を `codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/` に **extracted npm tarball contents + 記録された tarball sha256** で固定 (`.tgz` ファイルは worktree にコミットしない方針、`tarball-checksums.txt` で sha256 のみ pin) | [turnkey-source-pins.md](../codex-crypto-reviews/turnkey-source-pins.md) |
   158	| Tier-1 hand-transcribed fixtures | `tests/Fixtures/{encoding,crypto,api-key-stamper}/turnkey-*-vectors.json` の 3 ファイル。`_provenance` メタデータと `_source_line` 付き | `tests/Fixtures/http/` は**未整備** |
   159	| 3-round Codex review | 6 ファイル全部 review-clean、`FINAL-INTEGRATED-REVIEW-20260523.md` で v0.1.0-alpha GO 済み | [FINAL-INTEGRATED-REVIEW-20260523.md](../codex-crypto-reviews/FINAL-INTEGRATED-REVIEW-20260523.md) |
   160	| C# test 数 (合計約 113 `[Fact]/[Theory]`) | Encoding 48 / Crypto ~45 / Stamper 10 / Http 11 | 公式 (~30 `test()`) より細かいが、対応マッピングは未文書化 |
   161	| Drift 検知 | `tarball-checksums.txt` のみ。`__tests__/*.ts` 自体の sha256 pin は無し | 公式テスト更新時に気付かないリスク |
   162	| Node 生成 byte fixture | **なし** (`tests/Fixtures/Generators/` 未作成) | `Tier-1 README.md` に「node-generated 予定」と明記済み |
   163	| RFC / NIST vectors | HKDF RFC 5869 A1-A3 のみ (`tests/CryptoTests.cs:91/111/149`) | HPKE 9180、ECDSA 6979 単独、AES-GCM CAVP は未取り込み |
   164	
   165	### 公式テストの実状 (2026-05-27 時点・調査済み)
   166	
   167	公式 `__tests__/*.ts` は **`__fixtures__/api-key.{private,public,public.pem}`**
   168	というローカルファイルを `readFixture()` で読む構造で、
   169	他言語に直接持ち込める JSON 形式の test vector dataset は**公開されていない**。
   170	npm tarball にはテストもフィクスチャも含まれないため、
   171	**GitHub の `tkhq/sdk` リポジトリの該当タグからコピーする**のが唯一の入口。
   172	これは既存の `upstream-snapshots/.../ts-source/__fixtures__/` で対応済み。
   173	
   174	公式テストの assertion 強度は (1) DER ECDSA 検証 + (2) スキーム文字列 +
   175	(3) JSON キー順 + (4) publicKey 等価 のみ。**バイト等価 snapshot は無い**
   176	(P-256 `nodecrypto.ts` は random-k なため bytes が毎回変わる)。
   177	したがって C# 側で「`purejs` 等価のバイト」を追加で検証することは、
   178	**公式テストより厳しい superset の検証**になる (=価値が高い)。
   179	
   180	#### 公式他言語 SDK の検証スタイル (調査結果)
   181	
   182	- **cross-language fixture セットは存在しない**。
   183	  代わりに `mockSenderPrivateKey="67ee05fc..."`、
   184	  `mockPrivateKey="20fa65df..."`、`mockCredentialBundle="w99a5xV6..."`、
   185	  ニーモニック `"leaf lady until indicate praise final route toast cake minimum insect unknown"`、
   186	  PEM 鍵 `487f361d…0213c` / 圧縮公開鍵 `02f739f8…0316` が
   187	  **`tkhq/sdk` / `swift-sdk` / `dart-sdk` の 3 レポで完全一致のコピー**で
   188	  共有されており、実質的な reference vector になっている。
   189	  → C# でも同じ hex / mnemonic を使えば、3 言語と機械的に三角検証できる。
   190	- **`tkhq/sdk/packages/crypto/src/__tests__/proof-tests.ts`** には
   191	  **実 enclave が発行した複数の `v1AppProof` / `v1BootProof` JSON**
   192	  がフルで埋め込み済。署名検証ロジックの cross-language ゴールデン
   193	  として現状最高品質。
   194	- **`tkhq/go-sdk/pkg/enclave_encrypt/encrypt_test.go::TestP256Verify`**
   195	  は `// Values generated by rust code` コメント付きの **Go↔Rust の
   196	  cross-language ECDSA vector**。「ある言語の出力を別言語の入力に使う」
   197	  という稀有な明示例。
   198	- **`tkhq/qos/src/qos_p256/SPEC.md`** は **QOS encryption の独自仕様書**
   199	  (SDK HPKE とは別経路。Section 2.1 参照)。
   200	  ECDH(P-256) → HMAC-SHA512 で AES-GCM-256 の key を派生、
   201	  `QOS_ENCRYPTION_HMAC_MESSAGE` 定数、nonce 12B など、
   202	  **RFC 9180 とは互換性のない独自構成**。
   203	  C# は QOS をポートしておらず本プラン scope 外。
   204	- 公式 backend に対する live e2e を CI に組み込んでいるのは
   205	  `tkhq/python-sdk` のみ。他はすべて mocked。
   206	
   207	## 4. 既存の検証ギャップ (Why this plan)
   208	
   209	GAP-1. **Coverage matrix 不在** — 公式 `test("...")` と C# `[Fact]` Method の
   210	       対応表が無く、公式が test を追加したときに C# 側で漏れる。
   211	GAP-2. **HTTP fixture 不在** — `tests/Fixtures/http/turnkey-http-vectors.json`
   212	       が無い ([Http.cs-codex-findings-reconciliation.md セクション F](../codex-crypto-reviews/Http.cs-codex-findings-reconciliation.md))。
   213	GAP-3. **Node 生成バイト fixture 不在** — `Generators/` 機構が無いので
   214	       `purejs` モードで実 Node が吐く DER 署名や `SignedRequest.body`
   215	       バイトと C# 出力を比較できない。
   216	GAP-4. **Drift 検知 (テスト側) 不在** — `__tests__/*.ts` 自体の sha256 が
   217	       pin されていない。上流テスト更新を catch できない。
   218	GAP-5. **Primitive 単独ベクトル不足** — HKDF 以外 (ECDSA P-256 RFC 6979 単独・
   219	       AES-GCM-256 NIST CAVP・HMAC-SHA256 RFC 4231・SHA-256 NIST SHS・
   220	       Ed25519 RFC 8032・secp256k1 SEC2・Base58Check Bitcoin double-SHA256) の
   221	       単体テストが無い。SDK HPKE 全体 (RFC 9180 互換性は未確認、Section 2.1 参照)
   222	       の取り込みは PR-7a の評価結果次第とし、それまでは primitives 単独ベクトル
   223	       でカバーする。
   224	GAP-6. **proof モジュール非対応** — `crypto/proof.ts` (129 行) と
   225	       `proof-tests.ts` (実 enclave 由来の JSON ゴールデン) が C# に
   226	       存在しない。**proof のポート要否は別計画**だが、本プランでは
   227	       「ゴールデン JSON を Fixture 側に取り込む準備」 (実コード非実装) は
   228	       含める。proof 検証は ECDSA P-256 + base64url 復号で実現できるため、
   229	       既存 C# プリミティブで verify ロジックだけ書ける見込みが立つかは
   230	       別プランで判定する。
   231	GAP-7. **他言語 SDK との同名 hex 値共有が活用されていない** —
   232	       `mockSenderPrivateKey` 等の同名定数が 3 言語で完全一致。
   233	       これを C# 側でも採用すれば三角検証ができるが、現状ローカルで
   234	       別の値を生成しているテストがある (例: `Hpke_EncryptThenDecrypt_RoundTripsArbitraryPayload`)。
   235	
   236	## 5. 検証戦略 (4 Tier)
   237	
   238	```
   239	Tier 1: Upstream-transcribed JSON vectors    [PARTIAL — encoding/crypto/stamper のみ]
   240	        ↑ どこから来た値か Provenance 必須
   241	Tier 2: Node-generated byte snapshots        [NEW]
   242	        ↑ 公式 npm を実 Node で動かして固定。`purejs` ランタイム選択
   243	Tier 3: Standard RFC / NIST vectors          [NEW (HKDF を除き)]
   244	        ↑ 上流が間違うリスクの保険
   245	Tier 4: Live backend (opt-in)                [既存スキップ条件付き]
   246	        ↑ env 変数があるときのみ
   247	```
   248	
   249	各 Tier の **provenance** を `tests/Fixtures/README.md` のレベル分類
   250	(`upstream-test-vectors` / `node-generated` / `rfc` / `nist` /
   251	`turnkey-sample`) で必ず明示する。
   252	
   253	## 6. 設計 — コンポーネント分解
   254	
   255	### 6.1 Coverage matrix generator (新規)
   256	
   257	**目的**: 公式 `__tests__/*.ts` の `test()/it()` ブロック名一覧と、
   258	C# テストの `[Fact]` メソッド名一覧をクロス参照し、対応表を生成する。
   259	
   260	**実装案**: TypeScript ではなく **POSIX `awk` + dotnet test 一覧** のシェル

   603

   605	2. `codex-crypto-reviews/coverage-map.sh --check` が exit 0

   608	   または **同じ open issue で update され続けている** 状態)。
   609	4. `FINAL-INTEGRATED-REVIEW-*.md` の更新版が同条件で再 GO。
   610	5. README "Verification posture" 章が **PR-14 で更新され main にマージ済み**。

   612	   **decrypt round-trip 等価 + 構造的 assertion パス**。

   616	
   617	| リスク | 対策 |
   618	|---|---|
   619	| `purejs` runtime と `nodecrypto.ts` runtime の signature byte 差 | PR-5/6 では `runtimeOverride: "purejs"` を必ず指定。doc にも明記。さらに generator pre-flight で既知 vector check |
   620	| Node version drift で fixture が再生成毎に変わる | `package-lock.json` を commit、`node_version` を fixture に記録、generator が `process.version` を起動時 assert |

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	#!/usr/bin/env bash
     2	#
     3	# coverage-map.sh — generate / verify the upstream test → C# test coverage matrix.
     4	#
     5	# Modes:
     6	#   coverage-map.sh           — write coverage-map.tsv + coverage-map.md (no gate)
     7	#   coverage-map.sh --check   — write outputs AND exit non-zero if any
     8	#                                upstream test is MISSING from C# coverage and
     9	#                                has no N/A reason recorded in coverage-map.na.tsv.
    10	#
    11	# Inputs:
    12	#   codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/*/ts-source/__tests__/*-test*.ts
    13	#                                 — upstream test files (extracted npm tarball,
    14	#                                   not the test() blocks inside compiled output)
    15	#   tests/*Tests.cs              — C# test files. Each test method's coverage is
    16	#                                  declared by an XML doc-comment of the form:
    17	#                                    /// upstream: <relpath>:<line> "<test name>"
    18	#                                  placed immediately above the [Fact]/[Theory]
    19	#                                  attribute. The annotation is hand-maintained.
    20	#   codex-crypto-reviews/coverage-map.na.tsv
    21	#                                 — manually-curated rows for upstream tests that
    22	#                                  the C# SDK deliberately does NOT port. Each
    23	#                                  row is TAB-separated:
    24	#                                    <upstream_relpath>:<line><TAB><reason>
    25	#                                  The reason MUST be non-empty (the gate rejects
    26	#                                  empty reasons).
    27	#
    28	# Outputs:
    29	#   codex-crypto-reviews/coverage-map.tsv
    30	#                                 — joined matrix, one row per upstream test.
    31	#   codex-crypto-reviews/coverage-map.md
    32	#                                 — same data rendered for human review.
    33	
    34	set -euo pipefail
    35	
    36	REPO_ROOT="$(cd "$(dirname "$0")/.." && pwd)"
    37	REVIEWS_DIR="$REPO_ROOT/codex-crypto-reviews"
    38	UPSTREAM_DIR="$REVIEWS_DIR/upstream-snapshots"
    39	TESTS_DIR="$REPO_ROOT/tests"
    40	NA_FILE="$REVIEWS_DIR/coverage-map.na.tsv"
    41	TSV_OUT="$REVIEWS_DIR/coverage-map.tsv"
    42	MD_OUT="$REVIEWS_DIR/coverage-map.md"
    43	
    44	CHECK_MODE=0
    45	if [[ "${1:-}" == "--check" ]]; then
    46	  CHECK_MODE=1
    47	fi
    48	
    49	cd "$REPO_ROOT"
    50	
    51	# -------------------------------------------------------------------
    52	# Step 1. Enumerate upstream tests.
    53	#
    54	# Format emitted to TMP_UPSTREAM (TAB-separated):
    55	#   <relpath>:<line>\t<test-name>
    56	#
    57	# Handles two source forms:
    58	#   (a) test("name", ...)            — single-string test()/it()
    59	#   (b) test.each([...])("name", …)  — parametrized; name template can contain $var
    60	# -------------------------------------------------------------------
    61	
    62	TMP_UPSTREAM="$(mktemp)"
    63	trap 'rm -f "$TMP_UPSTREAM" "$TMP_MAPPED" "$TMP_NA" "$TMP_REPORT" 2>/dev/null || true' EXIT
    64	TMP_MAPPED="$(mktemp)"
    65	TMP_NA="$(mktemp)"
    66	TMP_REPORT="$(mktemp)"
    67	
    68	# Use find -print0 + xargs is safer for spaces but our path tree has no spaces.
    69	# Keep simple: glob expansion with sorted ordering.
    70	UPSTREAM_FILES=()
    71	while IFS= read -r f; do
    72	  UPSTREAM_FILES+=("$f")
    73	done < <(find "$UPSTREAM_DIR" -type f \
    74	            \( -name '*-test.ts' -o -name '*-tests.ts' \) \
    75	            -path '*/__tests__/*' | sort)
    76	
    77	for f in "${UPSTREAM_FILES[@]}"; do
    78	  rel="${f#$REPO_ROOT/}"
    79	  awk -v rel="$rel" '
    80	    BEGIN { in_each=0; each_line=0 }
    81	    # match "test(" / "it(" with a literal-string first argument
    82	    /^[[:space:]]*(test|it)[[:space:]]*\(["'"'"']/ {
    83	      line=NR
    84	      # extract quoted name. allow either " or '"'"'
    85	      s=$0
    86	      sub(/^[[:space:]]*(test|it)[[:space:]]*\(["'"'"']/, "", s)
    87	      # cut at trailing matching quote — heuristic: last "," is the arg sep
    88	      # so split at the last ", " preceding "(" / "=>"
    89	      # simpler: cut at first unescaped trailing quote followed by comma
    90	      n=index(s, "\","); if (n==0) n=index(s, "'"'"',")
    91	      if (n>0) {
    92	        name=substr(s, 1, n-1)
    93	      } else {
    94	        # fallback: strip leading quote, take until next quote
    95	        name=s
    96	        sub(/["'"'"'].*$/, "", name)
    97	      }
    98	      printf("%s:%d\t%s\n", rel, line, name)
    99	      next
   100	    }
   101	    # match "test.each([" / "it.each([" — record the line; the template comes
   102	    # on a later line and looks like:  ])("template", …)
   103	    /^[[:space:]]*(test|it)\.each[[:space:]]*\([[:space:]]*\[/ {
   104	      in_each=1; each_line=NR; next
   105	    }
   106	    in_each && /^[[:space:]]*\]\)[[:space:]]*\(["'"'"']/ {
   107	      s=$0
   108	      sub(/^[[:space:]]*\]\)[[:space:]]*\(["'"'"']/, "", s)
   109	      n=index(s, "\","); if (n==0) n=index(s, "'"'"',")
   110	      if (n>0) name=substr(s,1,n-1); else { name=s; sub(/["'"'"'].*$/, "", name) }
   111	      printf("%s:%d\t%s\n", rel, each_line, name)
   112	      in_each=0
   113	      next
   114	    }
   115	  ' "$f"
   116	done > "$TMP_UPSTREAM"
   117	
   118	# -------------------------------------------------------------------
   119	# Step 2. Enumerate C# test annotations.
   120	#
   121	# Find every line of form:
   122	#   /// upstream: <relpath>:<line> "<name>"
   123	# and pair it with the closest following [Fact]/[Theory] + method.
   124	#
   125	# Output format (TAB-separated):
   126	#   <relpath>:<line>\t<cs-file>:<cs-line>\t<cs-method>
   127	# -------------------------------------------------------------------
   128	
   129	for f in "$TESTS_DIR"/*Tests.cs; do
   130	  [ -f "$f" ] || continue
   131	  rel="${f#$REPO_ROOT/}"
   132	  awk -v csfile="$rel" '
   133	    function reset_pending() { delete pending; pending_n=0 }
   134	    BEGIN { pending_n=0 }
   135	    /^[[:space:]]*\/\/\/[[:space:]]*upstream:[[:space:]]/ {
   136	      # parse: /// upstream: <key> [..."<name>"]
   137	      # capture the first space-delimited token after "upstream:"
   138	      s=$0
   139	      sub(/^[[:space:]]*\/\/\/[[:space:]]*upstream:[[:space:]]*/, "", s)
   140	      # split by whitespace, take first field as the key
   141	      n=split(s, parts, /[[:space:]]+/)
   142	      key=parts[1]
   143	      pending_n++
   144	      pending[pending_n]=key
   145	      next
   146	    }
   147	    /^[[:space:]]*public[[:space:]]+(async[[:space:]]+)?(void|Task)[[:space:]]+[A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*[[:space:]]*\(/ {
   148	      if (pending_n > 0) {
   149	        s=$0
   150	        sub(/^[[:space:]]*public[[:space:]]+(async[[:space:]]+)?(void|Task)[[:space:]]+/, "", s)
   151	        sub(/[[:space:]]*\(.*$/, "", s)
   152	        for (i=1; i<=pending_n; i++) {
   153	          printf("%s\t%s:%d\t%s\n", pending[i], csfile, NR, s)
   154	        }
   155	        reset_pending()
   156	      }
   157	      next
   158	    }
   159	    # If we see a non-comment non-attribute line before the public decl,
   160	    # drop any pending annotations (defensive: prevents drift if a /// upstream
   161	    # comment sits orphaned at the end of a region without a matching method).
   162	    /^[[:space:]]*\}/ && pending_n > 0 { reset_pending() }
   163	  ' "$f"
   164	done > "$TMP_MAPPED"
   165	
   166	# -------------------------------------------------------------------
   167	# Step 3. Load N/A entries.
   168	# -------------------------------------------------------------------
   169	
   170	if [ -f "$NA_FILE" ]; then
   171	  awk -F '\t' '
   172	    /^[[:space:]]*#/ { next }
   173	    NF == 0 { next }
   174	    {
   175	      key=$1
   176	      reason=$2
   177	      printf("%s\t%s\n", key, reason)
   178	    }
   179	  ' "$NA_FILE" > "$TMP_NA"
   180	else
   181	  : > "$TMP_NA"
   182	fi
   183	
   184	# -------------------------------------------------------------------
   185	# Step 4. Join — emit one row per upstream test.
   186	#
   187	# TSV columns (header on row 1):
   188	#   upstream_key  upstream_name  status  csharp_file  csharp_line  csharp_method  reason
   189	# -------------------------------------------------------------------
   190	
   191	{
   192	  printf "upstream_key\tupstream_name\tstatus\tcsharp_target\tcsharp_method\treason\n"
   193	  awk -F '\t' \
   194	      -v mapped="$TMP_MAPPED" \
   195	      -v na="$TMP_NA" '
   196	    function load_mapped() {
   197	      while ((getline line < mapped) > 0) {
   198	        n=split(line, p, "\t")
   199	        if (n >= 3) {
   200	          k=p[1]
   201	          # store comma-separated list of cs targets
   202	          if (k in mapk) {
   203	            mapk[k] = mapk[k] ", " p[2] " " p[3]
   204	          } else {
   205	            mapk[k] = p[2] " " p[3]
   206	          }
   207	        }
   208	      }
   209	      close(mapped)
   210	    }
   211	    function load_na() {
   212	      while ((getline line < na) > 0) {
   213	        n=split(line, p, "\t")
   214	        if (n >= 2) {
   215	          nak[p[1]] = p[2]
   216	        }
   217	      }
   218	      close(na)
   219	    }
   220	    BEGIN { load_mapped(); load_na() }
   221	    {
   222	      key=$1; name=$2
   223	      status="MISSING"; tgt=""; meth=""; reason=""
   224	      if (key in mapk) {
   225	        status="REVIEWED"
   226	        tgt=mapk[key]
   227	      } else if (key in nak) {
   228	        status="N/A"
   229	        reason=nak[key]
   230	      }
   231	      # split cs_target back into file vs method for the tsv output
   232	      if (status == "REVIEWED") {
   233	        n=split(tgt, parts, " ")
   234	        printf("%s\t%s\t%s\t%s\t%s\t\n", key, name, status, parts[1], parts[2])
   235	      } else {
   236	        printf("%s\t%s\t%s\t\t\t%s\n", key, name, status, reason)
   237	      }
   238	    }
   239	  ' "$TMP_UPSTREAM"
   240	} > "$TSV_OUT"
   241	
   242	# -------------------------------------------------------------------
   243	# Step 5. Render markdown.
   244	# -------------------------------------------------------------------
   245	
   246	{
   247	  echo "# Coverage map — upstream test ↔ C# test"
   248	  echo ""
   249	  echo "Generated by [\`coverage-map.sh\`](./coverage-map.sh)."
   250	  echo ""
   251	  echo "Statuses:"
   252	  echo ""
   253	  echo "- **REVIEWED** — at least one C# \`[Fact]/[Theory]\` method has a"
   254	  echo "  matching \`/// upstream: <relpath>:<line>\` annotation."
   255	  echo "- **N/A** — the upstream test is intentionally not ported; the reason"
   256	  echo "  is recorded in [\`coverage-map.na.tsv\`](./coverage-map.na.tsv)."
   257	  echo "- **MISSING** — neither of the above. PR-3 must either add C# coverage"
   258	  echo "  or add an explicit N/A row with a non-empty reason."
   259	  echo ""
   260	  echo "## Summary"
   261	  echo ""
   262	  awk -F '\t' 'NR>1 { c[$3]++ } END { for (k in c) printf("- %s: %d\n", k, c[k]) }' "$TSV_OUT" | sort
   263	  echo ""
   264	  echo "## Rows"
   265	  echo ""
   266	  echo "| Upstream key | Upstream test name | Status | C# target | C# method | N/A reason |"
   267	  echo "|---|---|---|---|---|---|"
   268	  awk -F '\t' 'NR>1 {
   269	    # escape pipes in names just in case
   270	    for (i=1; i<=NF; i++) gsub(/\|/, "\\|", $i)
   271	    printf("| `%s` | %s | %s | %s | %s | %s |\n", $1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6)
   272	  }' "$TSV_OUT"
   273	} > "$MD_OUT"
   274	
   275	# -------------------------------------------------------------------
   276	# Step 6. --check mode: enforce gate.
   277	# -------------------------------------------------------------------
   278	
   279	if [ "$CHECK_MODE" = "1" ]; then
   280	  exit_code=0
   281	  # any MISSING ?
   282	  if awk -F '\t' 'NR>1 && $3=="MISSING" { print; found=1 } END { exit found?1:0 }' "$TSV_OUT" >/dev/null; then
   283	    : # awk exit 0 means no missing
   284	  else
   285	    echo "ERROR: MISSING rows detected. See $TSV_OUT or $MD_OUT."
   286	    awk -F '\t' 'NR>1 && $3=="MISSING" { print "  MISSING: " $1 "  " $2 }' "$TSV_OUT"
   287	    exit_code=1
   288	  fi
   289	  # any N/A with empty reason ?
   290	  if awk -F '\t' 'NR>1 && $3=="N/A" && ($6=="" || $6 ~ /^[[:space:]]*$/) { print; found=1 } END { exit found?1:0 }' "$TSV_OUT" >/dev/null; then
   291	    :
   292	  else
   293	    echo "ERROR: N/A rows missing reason text:"
   294	    awk -F '\t' 'NR>1 && $3=="N/A" && ($6=="" || $6 ~ /^[[:space:]]*$/) { print "  EMPTY-NA-REASON: " $1 "  " $2 }' "$TSV_OUT"
   295	    exit_code=1
   296	  fi
   297	  if [ "$exit_code" = "0" ]; then
   298	    echo "coverage-map check passed: 0 MISSING, all N/A rows have reasons."
   299	  fi
   300	  exit "$exit_code"
   301	fi
   302	
   303	# Default mode prints a short summary to stderr so CI logs are readable.
   304	{
   305	  echo "Wrote $TSV_OUT"
   306	  echo "Wrote $MD_OUT"
   307	  awk -F '\t' 'NR>1 { c[$3]++ } END { for (k in c) printf("  %s: %d\n", k, c[k]) }' "$TSV_OUT" | sort
   308	} 1>&2

/bin/zsh -lc "nl -ba .github/workflows/upstream-drift.yml | sed -n '1,280p'" in /Users/takeshi/Kyuzan/src/turnkey-sdk-csharp/.claude/worktrees/laughing-hertz-048cd4
 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	# Upstream-drift detection (idempotent).
     2	#
     3	# Once a month, hash each pinned upstream __tests__/*.ts and
     4	# __fixtures__/* file at the pinned git tag SHA via the GitHub
     5	# Contents API, then compare to the local pin in
     6	# codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/test-file-checksums.txt.
     7	#
     8	# Per plan Section 6.4 and Section 9 risk row "公式テストファイル
     9	# sha256 を pin したのに毎月差分が出て CI が騒がしい":
    10	#
    11	#   - This workflow is NOT a main-branch CI gate. It can never block
    12	#     a PR. Drift surfaces only as a GitHub issue.
    13	#   - Issue creation is idempotent: at most ONE open issue with the
    14	#     `upstream-drift` label and the package name in the title. A
    15	#     re-detected drift updates the body and posts a re-detection
    16	#     comment instead of opening a duplicate.
    17	#
    18	# Manual trigger via workflow_dispatch is supported so reviewers can
    19	# re-run after re-pinning without waiting for the next cron tick.
    20	
    21	name: Upstream drift detection
    22	
    23	on:
    24	  workflow_dispatch:
    25	  schedule:
    26	    - cron: "0 8 1 * *"  # 1st of each month, 08:00 UTC
    27	
    28	permissions:
    29	  contents: read
    30	  issues: write
    31	
    32	jobs:
    33	  drift:
    34	    name: Drift detection (${{ matrix.package }})
    35	    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    36	    strategy:
    37	      fail-fast: false
    38	      matrix:
    39	        include:
    40	          - package: turnkey-crypto-2.8.8
    41	            owner: tkhq
    42	            repo: sdk
    43	            git_tag_sha: b35dc642bd7c1728f97acd43d4cba66976b65084
    44	            tarball_dir: packages/crypto
    45	          - package: turnkey-http-3.16.0
    46	            owner: tkhq
    47	            repo: sdk
    48	            git_tag_sha: 8def9ba521233137437ac7294693a4ae0a0d14da
    49	            tarball_dir: packages/http
    50	          - package: turnkey-api-key-stamper-0.5.0
    51	            owner: tkhq
    52	            repo: sdk
    53	            git_tag_sha: b711befbb88ec522452dbdac68f0e98762be10dd
    54	            tarball_dir: packages/api-key-stamper
    55	          - package: turnkey-encoding-0.6.0
    56	            owner: tkhq
    57	            repo: sdk
    58	            git_tag_sha: 60a997f4c52ac5f98bdd285af934f02699b88bff
    59	            tarball_dir: packages/encoding
    60	    steps:
    61	      - uses: actions/checkout@v6
    62	
    63	      # The pin file format is "<sha256>  <relpath>" where <relpath>
    64	      # always starts with "codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/".
    65	      # We need to convert that to the GitHub Contents API path which
    66	      # is "<tarball_dir>/src/__tests__/<file>" — the live upstream
    67	      # GitHub tree does not have a "ts-source" prefix.
    68	      #
    69	      # Concretely the local path looks like:
    70	      #   codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/turnkey-crypto-2.8.8/ts-source/__tests__/crypto-test.ts
    71	      # and the upstream path is:
    72	      #   packages/crypto/src/__tests__/crypto-test.ts
    73	      #
    74	      # The mapping is per-package because monorepo layouts vary.
    75	      - name: Compute drift report
    76	        id: drift
    77	        env:
    78	          GH_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
    79	          PACKAGE: ${{ matrix.package }}
    80	          OWNER: ${{ matrix.owner }}
    81	          REPO: ${{ matrix.repo }}
    82	          GIT_SHA: ${{ matrix.git_tag_sha }}
    83	          TARBALL_DIR: ${{ matrix.tarball_dir }}
    84	        run: |
    85	          set -euo pipefail
    86	
    87	          REPORT=$(mktemp)
    88	          : > "$REPORT"
    89	
    90	          drift_count=0
    91	
    92	          while IFS= read -r line; do
    93	            # Skip comments and blank lines.
    94	            [[ -z "${line// }" ]] && continue
    95	            [[ "$line" =~ ^# ]] && continue
    96	
    97	            # Format: "<sha256>  <relpath>"
    98	            expected_sha=$(awk '{print $1}' <<<"$line")
    99	            relpath=$(awk '{print $2}' <<<"$line")
   100	
   101	            # Filter to this matrix package only.
   102	            case "$relpath" in
   103	              "codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/${PACKAGE}/"*) ;;
   104	              *) continue ;;
   105	            esac
   106	
   107	            # Strip the local prefix to derive the in-tarball relative path,
   108	            # then rewrite "ts-source" -> "src" for the live upstream layout.
   109	            local_subpath="${relpath#codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/${PACKAGE}/}"
   110	            upstream_subpath=${local_subpath/ts-source\//src/}
   111	
   112	            # Read the live file via the Contents API at the pinned SHA.
   113	            api_path="repos/${OWNER}/${REPO}/contents/${TARBALL_DIR}/${upstream_subpath}?ref=${GIT_SHA}"
   114	            live_b64=$(gh api -H "Accept: application/vnd.github+json" "$api_path" --jq '.content // ""')
   115	            if [[ -z "$live_b64" ]]; then
   116	              {
   117	                echo "- **MISSING_UPSTREAM**: \`${upstream_subpath}\` (not found at ${OWNER}/${REPO}@${GIT_SHA})";
   118	              } >> "$REPORT"
   119	              drift_count=$((drift_count + 1))
   120	              continue
   121	            fi
   122	
   123	            # Contents API base64-decodes with embedded newlines.
   124	            live_sha=$(printf '%s' "$live_b64" | tr -d '\n' | base64 -d | shasum -a 256 | awk '{print $1}')
   125	
   126	            if [[ "$live_sha" != "$expected_sha" ]]; then
   127	              {
   128	                echo "- **DRIFT**: \`${upstream_subpath}\``"
   129	                echo "  - expected sha256 \`${expected_sha}\``"
   130	                echo "  - live sha256     \`${live_sha}\``"
   131	                echo "  - live ref        \`${OWNER}/${REPO}@${GIT_SHA}\``"
   132	              } >> "$REPORT"
   133	              drift_count=$((drift_count + 1))
   134	            fi
   135	          done < codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/test-file-checksums.txt
   136	
   137	          {
   138	            echo "DRIFT_COUNT=$drift_count"
   139	            echo "REPORT_PATH=$REPORT"
   140	          } >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
   141	
   142	      # Idempotent issue handling (plan Section 6.4):
   143	      #   - Search for an open issue labelled `upstream-drift` whose
   144	      #     title contains the package name.
   145	      #   - If found: edit the body to the latest report and add a
   146	      #     re-detection comment with the timestamp.
   147	      #   - If not found: open a new issue.
   148	      #   - If drift_count is 0 and an open issue exists: close it
   149	      #     with a "resolved" comment.
   150	      - name: Upsert drift issue
   151	        if: always()
   152	        env:
   153	          GH_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
   154	          DRIFT_LABEL: upstream-drift
   155	          PACKAGE: ${{ matrix.package }}
   156	          DRIFT_COUNT: ${{ steps.drift.outputs.DRIFT_COUNT }}
   157	          REPORT_PATH: ${{ steps.drift.outputs.REPORT_PATH }}
   158	        run: |
   159	          set -euo pipefail
   160	
   161	          gh label create "$DRIFT_LABEL" --color "d73a4a" \
   162	            --description "Upstream test-file sha256 drift detected" 2>/dev/null || true
   163	
   164	          # Build the body up-front so the rest of the logic is single-shot.
   165	          if [[ "$DRIFT_COUNT" -gt 0 ]]; then
   166	            BODY_FILE=$(mktemp)
   167	            {
   168	              echo "Detected $DRIFT_COUNT drift row(s) for package \`$PACKAGE\` at $(date -u +%FT%TZ)."
   169	              echo ""
   170	              echo "## Drift"
   171	              echo ""
   172	              cat "$REPORT_PATH"
   173	              echo ""
   174	              echo "## Re-pin procedure"
   175	              echo ""
   176	              echo "See \`codex-crypto-reviews/turnkey-source-pins.md\` (\"Re-pinning procedure\")."
   177	            } > "$BODY_FILE"
   178	          fi
   179	
   180	          # Locate the single existing open issue (idempotent).
   181	          EXISTING=$(gh issue list \
   182	            --state open \
   183	            --label "$DRIFT_LABEL" \
   184	            --search "in:title $PACKAGE" \
   185	            --json number \
   186	            --jq '.[0].number // empty')
   187	
   188	          if [[ "$DRIFT_COUNT" -gt 0 ]]; then
   189	            if [[ -n "$EXISTING" ]]; then
   190	              gh issue edit "$EXISTING" --body-file "$BODY_FILE"
   191	              gh issue comment "$EXISTING" --body \
   192	                "Re-detected upstream drift on $(date -u +%FT%TZ)."
   193	            else
   194	              gh issue create \
   195	                --label "$DRIFT_LABEL" \
   196	                --title "Upstream drift: $PACKAGE" \
   197	                --body-file "$BODY_FILE"
   198	            fi
   199	          else
   200	            if [[ -n "$EXISTING" ]]; then
   201	              gh issue comment "$EXISTING" --body \
   202	                "Drift resolved (re-checked $(date -u +%FT%TZ))."
   203	              gh issue close "$EXISTING"
   204	            else
   205	              echo "No drift detected and no open issue. Nothing to do."
   206	            fi
   207	          fi

exec
/bin/zsh -lc "nl -ba tests/ApiKeyStamperTests.cs | sed -n '1,360p'" in /Users/takeshi/Kyuzan/src/turnkey-sdk-csharp/.claude/worktrees/laughing-hertz-048cd4
 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	// ApiKeyStamperTests.cs — xunit tests for src/ApiKeyStamper.cs.
     2	//
     3	// Vector sources:
     4	//   codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/turnkey-api-key-stamper-0.5.0/ts-source/__fixtures__/api-key.{private,public}
     5	//   codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/turnkey-api-key-stamper-0.5.0/ts-source/__tests__/stamp-test.ts
     6	//
     7	// P-256 ECDSA signatures are not deterministic across libraries (noble uses
     8	// RFC 6979; BouncyCastle's HMacDsaKCalculator also uses RFC 6979 with the
     9	// same digest, so for identical input + key + nonce-source the signature
    10	// is deterministic). Tests therefore assert:
    11	//   - the header name == "X-Stamp"
    12	//   - the base64url-decoded JSON has keys ["publicKey", "scheme", "signature"]
    13	//   - publicKey matches the configured key
    14	//   - scheme == "SIGNATURE_SCHEME_TK_API_P256"
    15	//   - the signature is a valid DER-encoded ECDSA signature over SHA-256(content)
    16	//     under the configured public key
    17	
    18	using System;
    19	using System.IO;
    20	using System.Text;
    21	using System.Text.Json;
    22	using FluentAssertions;
    23	using Org.BouncyCastle.Asn1;
    24	using Org.BouncyCastle.Asn1.X9;
    25	using Org.BouncyCastle.Crypto.Parameters;
    26	using Org.BouncyCastle.Math;
    27	using Org.BouncyCastle.Security;
    28	using Xunit;
    29	
    30	namespace Turnkey.Tests

    44	            // assigns fields; validation happens at sign time. C# mirrors
    45	            // that, including null tolerance.
    46	            Action act = () => new ApiKeyStamper(FixturePublicKey, "abcd");
    47	            act.Should().NotThrow();
    48	            Action act2 = () => new ApiKeyStamper(null!, null!);
    49	            act2.Should().NotThrow();
    50	        }

    54	        {

    56	            var stamper = new ApiKeyStamper(FixturePublicKey, "abcd");
    57	            Action act = () => stamper.SignWithApiKey("payload");
    58	            act.Should().Throw<ArgumentException>()
    59	               .WithMessage("invalid P-256 private key: expected 32 bytes, got 2");
    60	        }

    67	            Action act = () => stamper.SignWithApiKey("payload");
    68	            act.Should().Throw<ArgumentException>()
    69	               .WithMessage("invalid P-256 private key: scalar must be in [1, n - 1]");
    70	        }

    72	        /// upstream: codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/turnkey-api-key-stamper-0.5.0/ts-source/__tests__/stamp-test.ts:6 "uses provided signature to make stamp"
    73	        [Fact]
    74	        public void Stamp_UpstreamFixture_ProducesValidWireBytes()
    75	        {
    76	            // Matches upstream __tests__/stamp-test.ts:6-37
    77	            var stamper = new ApiKeyStamper(FixturePublicKey, FixturePrivateKey);
    78	            const string messageToSign = "hello from TKHQ!";
    79	
    80	            var result = stamper.Stamp(messageToSign);
    81	
    82	            result.StampHeaderName.Should().Be("X-Stamp");
    83	
    84	            // Decode base64url -> JSON -> object.
    85	            string decodedJson = Encoding.DecodeBase64UrlToString(result.StampHeaderValue);
    86	
    87	            using var doc = JsonDocument.Parse(decodedJson);
    88	            var root = doc.RootElement;
    89	
    90	            // Keys must be exactly publicKey, scheme, signature in this order.
    91	            int i = 0;
    92	            string[] expectedKeys = { "publicKey", "scheme", "signature" };
    93	            foreach (var prop in root.EnumerateObject())
    94	            {
    95	                prop.Name.Should().Be(expectedKeys[i++]);
    96	            }
    97	            i.Should().Be(3);
    98	
    99	            root.GetProperty("publicKey").GetString().Should().Be(FixturePublicKey);
   100	            root.GetProperty("scheme").GetString().Should().Be("SIGNATURE_SCHEME_TK_API_P256");
   101	
   102	            // Verify the DER ECDSA signature against SHA-256(content) under the
   103	            // public key. This is the wire-format gate: if the signature isn't
   104	            // verifiable against the configured P-256 key, the stamp would be
   105	            // rejected by Turnkey's backend.
   106	            string signatureHex = root.GetProperty("signature").GetString()!;
   107	            byte[] signatureBytes = HexToBytes(signatureHex);
   108	            AssertSignatureVerifies(FixturePublicKey, messageToSign, signatureBytes);
   109	        }

   112	        public void SignWithApiKey_ProducesDerHexThatVerifies()
   113	        {

   115	            const string content = "any payload we care to sign";
   116	            string sigHex = stamper.SignWithApiKey(content);
   117

   119	            (sigHex.Length % 2).Should().Be(0);
   120	            sigHex.Substring(0, 2).Should().Be("30");
   121	
   122	            AssertSignatureVerifies(FixturePublicKey, content, HexToBytes(sigHex));
   123	        }
   124	
   125	        [Fact]
   126	        public void SignWithApiKey_DeterministicWithRfc6979()
   127	        {
   128	            // RFC 6979 + same key + same content + same SHA-256(content) +
   129	            // same low-S normalization => signature is bit-identical across
   130	            // invocations (HMacDsaKCalculator is deterministic).
   131	            var stamper = new ApiKeyStamper(FixturePublicKey, FixturePrivateKey);
   132	            string a = stamper.SignWithApiKey("the same content");
   133	            string b = stamper.SignWithApiKey("the same content");
   134	            a.Should().Be(b);
   135	        }
   136	
   137	        [Fact]
   138	        public void SignWithApiKey_LowSEnforced()
   139	        {
   140	            // For RFC 6979 + low-S: the s value's high bit (top byte) must be
   141	            // strictly less than (n / 2 + 1). Verify by parsing the DER and
   142	            // checking the s integer is in the lower half of [1, n-1].
   143	            var stamper = new ApiKeyStamper(FixturePublicKey, FixturePrivateKey);
   144	            for (int i = 0; i < 8; i++)
   145	            {
   146	                string sigHex = stamper.SignWithApiKey("content_" + i);
   147	                var (r, s) = ParseDerEcdsa(HexToBytes(sigHex));
   148	
   149	                var curve = ECNamedCurveTable.GetByName(CryptoConstants.CURVE_NAME);
   150	                var halfN = curve.N.ShiftRight(1);
   151	                s.CompareTo(halfN).Should().BeLessOrEqualTo(0,
   152	                    "low-S requires s to be in (0, n/2]");
   153	                r.SignValue.Should().BeGreaterThan(0);
   154	                s.SignValue.Should().BeGreaterThan(0);
   155	            }
   156	        }
   157

   169	               .WithMessage("Bad API key. Expected to get public key*");
   170	        }

   183	            var result = stamper.Stamp("hello");

   188	                          || (c >= 'a' && c <= 'z')
   189	                          || (c >= '0' && c <= '9')
   190	                          || c == '-' || c == '_';

   192	            }

   195	        // ============================================================
   196	        // Node-generated byte fixture (PR-6, Tier-2)
   197	        //
   198	        // Loads tests/Fixtures/api-key-stamper/turnkey-stamper-node-vectors.json
   199	        // (produced by tests/Fixtures/Generators/generate-stamper-vectors.mjs)
   200	        // and confirms that for each upstream message:
   201	        //
   202	        //   1. C# stamper produces a stamp with the SAME publicKey,
   203	        //      SAME scheme, and SAME JSON key order as upstream.
   204	        //   2. C# stamper produces the SAME RFC 6979 deterministic r
   205	        //      value as upstream (the s value differs because C# enforces
   206	        //      low-S while upstream noble defaults to high-S; the
   207	        //      cryptographic equivalence is s' = n - s).
   208	        //   3. Both the upstream signature AND the C# signature verify
   209	        //      against the public key over SHA-256(message), proving
   210	        //      cryptographic equivalence.
   211	        //
   212	        // This is the "deterministic byte parity" gate for the stamper,
   213	        // expressed at the level where the two implementations agree.
   214	        // ============================================================
   215	
   216	        /// upstream: codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/turnkey-api-key-stamper-0.5.0/ts-source/__tests__/signature-test.ts:17 "sign with Turnkey fixture: sign (PureJS)"
   217	        [Fact]
   218	        public void NodeFixture_StamperByteParity_PureJsRfc6979()
   219	        {
   220	            // Resolve the fixture path. With CopyToOutputDirectory=PreserveNewest,
   221	            // the test runner copies the fixture next to the assembly.
   222	            string fixturePath = Path.Combine(
   223	                AppContext.BaseDirectory,
   224	                "Fixtures",
   225	                "api-key-stamper",
   226	                "turnkey-stamper-node-vectors.json");
   227	            File.Exists(fixturePath).Should().BeTrue(
   228	                "fixture must be committed by PR-6 and copied to output");
   229	
   230	            using var doc = JsonDocument.Parse(File.ReadAllText(fixturePath));
   231	            var root = doc.RootElement;
   232	
   233	            // Provenance sanity: must be node-generated with the pinned
   234	            // upstream package + a noble-curves 1.3.0 override.
   235	            var prov = root.GetProperty("_provenance");
   236	            prov.GetProperty("level").GetString().Should().Be("node-generated");
   237	            prov.GetProperty("runtime_override").GetString().Should().Be("purejs");
   238	
   239	            var preflight = root.GetProperty("preflight");
   240	            preflight.GetProperty("deterministic").GetBoolean().Should().BeTrue();
   241	            preflight.GetProperty("schemeOk").GetBoolean().Should().BeTrue();
   242	            preflight.GetProperty("keyOrderOk").GetBoolean().Should().BeTrue();
   243	
   244	            var stamps = root.GetProperty("stamps");
   245	            stamps.GetArrayLength().Should().BeGreaterThan(0);
   246	
   247	            foreach (var entry in stamps.EnumerateArray())
   248	            {
   249	                var input = entry.GetProperty("input");
   250	                string message = input.GetProperty("message").GetString()!;
   251	                string privHex = input.GetProperty("privateKey").GetString()!;
   252	                string pubHex = input.GetProperty("publicKey").GetString()!;
   253	
   254	                var expected = entry.GetProperty("expected");
   255	                string upstreamScheme = expected.GetProperty("decoded")
   256	                    .GetProperty("scheme").GetString()!;
   257	                string upstreamPublicKey = expected.GetProperty("decoded")
   258	                    .GetProperty("publicKey").GetString()!;
   259	                string upstreamSignatureDerHex = expected.GetProperty("decoded")
   260	                    .GetProperty("signature").GetString()!;
   261	
   262	                var derived = expected.GetProperty("derived");
   263	                string expectedRHex = derived.GetProperty("r_hex").GetString()!;
   264	                string expectedLowSHex =
   265	                    derived.GetProperty("low_s_equivalent_s_hex").GetString()!;
   266	
   267	                // C# stamper.
   268	                var stamper = new ApiKeyStamper(pubHex, privHex);
   269	                var stamp = stamper.Stamp(message);
   270	
   271	                stamp.StampHeaderName.Should().Be("X-Stamp");
   272	                string decodedJson = Encoding.DecodeBase64UrlToString(stamp.StampHeaderValue);
   273	                using var stampDoc = JsonDocument.Parse(decodedJson);
   274	                var stampRoot = stampDoc.RootElement;
   275	
   276	                // JSON key order: ["publicKey", "scheme", "signature"]
   277	                var propNames = new System.Collections.Generic.List<string>();
   278	                foreach (var p in stampRoot.EnumerateObject()) propNames.Add(p.Name);
   279	                propNames.Should().Equal("publicKey", "scheme", "signature");
   280	
   281	                stampRoot.GetProperty("publicKey").GetString().Should().Be(pubHex);
   282	                stampRoot.GetProperty("scheme").GetString().Should().Be(upstreamScheme);
   283	
   284	                string csSigHex = stampRoot.GetProperty("signature").GetString()!;
   285	                var (csR, csS) = ParseDerEcdsa(HexToBytes(csSigHex));
   286	                csR.ToString(16).TrimStart('0').Should().BeEquivalentTo(
   287	                    expectedRHex.TrimStart('0'),
   288	                    "C# RFC 6979 must derive the same k => same r as upstream");
   289	                csS.ToString(16).TrimStart('0').Should().BeEquivalentTo(
   290	                    expectedLowSHex.TrimStart('0'),
   291	                    "C# must emit the low-S form of upstream's high-S signature");
   292	
   293	                // Upstream's high-S sig and C# low-S sig both verify against
   294	                // the same public key over the same SHA-256(message).
   295	                AssertSignatureVerifies(pubHex, message, HexToBytes(upstreamSignatureDerHex));
   296	                AssertSignatureVerifies(pubHex, message, HexToBytes(csSigHex));
   297	
   298	                // The publicKey in the upstream and C# stamps must match
   299	                // exactly (independent of the s-form difference).
   300	                upstreamPublicKey.Should().Be(pubHex);
   301	            }
   302	        }
   303	
   304	        // ============================================================
   305	        // Helpers
   306	        // ============================================================
   307	
   308	        private static byte[] HexToBytes(string hex) => Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(hex);
   309	
   310	        private static void AssertSignatureVerifies(string compressedPubHex, string content, byte[] derSignature)
   311	        {
   312	            byte[] payloadBytes = System.Text.Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(content);
   313	
   314	            var digest = DigestUtilities.GetDigest("SHA-256");
   315	            digest.BlockUpdate(payloadBytes, 0, payloadBytes.Length);
   316	            var hash = new byte[digest.GetDigestSize()];
   317	            digest.DoFinal(hash, 0);
   318	
   319	            var curve = ECNamedCurveTable.GetByName(CryptoConstants.CURVE_NAME);
   320	            var domainParams = new ECDomainParameters(curve.Curve, curve.G, curve.N, curve.H, curve.GetSeed());
   321	
   322	            byte[] compressedPub = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(compressedPubHex);
   323	            var point = curve.Curve.DecodePoint(compressedPub);
   324	            var publicKey = new ECPublicKeyParameters(point, domainParams);
   325	
   326	            var signer = SignerUtilities.GetSigner("NONEwithECDSA");
   327	            signer.Init(false, publicKey);
   328	            signer.BlockUpdate(hash, 0, hash.Length);
   329	            signer.VerifySignature(derSignature).Should().BeTrue();
   330	        }
   331	
   332	        private static (BigInteger R, BigInteger S) ParseDerEcdsa(byte[] der)
   333	        {
   334	            using var ms = new MemoryStream(der);
   335	            using var reader = new Asn1InputStream(ms);
   336	            var seq = (DerSequence)reader.ReadObject();
   337	            var r = ((DerInteger)seq[0]).Value;
   338	            var s = ((DerInteger)seq[1]).Value;
   339	            return (r, s);
   340	        }
   341	    }
