/bin/zsh -lc "nl -ba tests/Fixtures/Generators/generate-stamper-vectors.mjs | sed -n '1,360p'" in /Users/takeshi/Kyuzan/src/turnkey-sdk-csharp/.claude/worktrees/laughing-hertz-048cd4
 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	// generate-stamper-vectors.mjs
     2	//
     3	// Produce deterministic stamper byte vectors by running pinned
     4	// @turnkey/api-key-stamper@0.5.0 with runtimeOverride="purejs" on the
     5	// pinned upstream fixture key pair.
     6	//
     7	// IMPORTANT DESIGN NOTE
     8	// ---------------------
     9	// Upstream purejs.ts (codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/
    10	//   turnkey-api-key-stamper-0.5.0/ts-source/purejs.ts) calls
    11	//   p256.sign(hash, privateKey)
    12	// with NO options. With every version of @noble/curves in the 1.x line
    13	// (1.3.0 through 1.9.x), this defaults to HIGH-S (s > n/2) — low-S
    14	// requires the explicit { lowS: true } option.
    15	//
    16	// The C# port (src/ApiKeyStamper.cs) enforces low-S because that is the
    17	// standard ECDSA wire-format that downstream verifiers expect. The two
    18	// signatures (HIGH-S vs LOW-S) are cryptographically equivalent under
    19	// the curve symmetry s ↔ (n - s) and BOTH verify against the same
    20	// public key.
    21	//
    22	// This generator therefore CANNOT byte-snapshot the upstream DER hex
    23	// (it would lock in HIGH-S, which the C# port would refuse to produce).
    24	// Instead it locks in everything that IS deterministic:
    25	//   - the r value (depends only on k from RFC 6979 — identical in both)
    26	//   - the publicKey embedded in the stamp (identical)
    27	//   - the scheme constant SIGNATURE_SCHEME_TK_API_P256 (identical)
    28	//   - the JSON key order ["publicKey", "scheme", "signature"] (identical)
    29	//   - the base64url stamp header value derivable from the above + the
    30	//     C# low-S signature
    31	//   - cryptographic verification: the C# stamper output must verify
    32	//     against the same public key, and so must this fixture's signature
    33	//
    34	// Both signatures must verify against the same hash + public key, so
    35	// the C# tests can compare r and verify the signature, but cannot
    36	// compare s or DER hex.
    37	//
    38	// This intentional divergence is documented as the load-bearing
    39	// finding from PR-4's preflight check (see plan Section 9 risk row
    40	// `@noble/curves transitive drift`).
    41	
    42	import { ApiKeyStamper } from "@turnkey/api-key-stamper";
    43	import { p256 } from "@noble/curves/p256";
    44	import { createHash } from "node:crypto";
    45	import { readFile, writeFile } from "node:fs/promises";
    46	import { execSync } from "node:child_process";
    47	import { fileURLToPath } from "node:url";
    48	import path from "node:path";
    49	
    50	const __filename = fileURLToPath(import.meta.url);
    51	const __dirname = path.dirname(__filename);
    52	const REPO_ROOT = path.resolve(__dirname, "..", "..", "..");
    53	const PREFLIGHT_ONLY = process.argv.includes("--preflight-only");
    54	
    55	const STAMPER_SNAPSHOT = path.join(
    56	  REPO_ROOT,
    57	  "codex-crypto-reviews",
    58	  "upstream-snapshots",
    59	  "turnkey-api-key-stamper-0.5.0",
    60	  "ts-source",
    61	  "__fixtures__",
    62	);
    63	
    64	const PREFLIGHT_PRIVATE = "487f361ddfd73440e707f4daa6775b376859e8a3c9f29b3bb694a12927c0213c";
    65	const PREFLIGHT_PUBLIC = "02f739f8c77b32f4d5f13265861febd76e7a9c61a1140d296b8c16302508870316";
    66	const PREFLIGHT_MESSAGE = "hello from TKHQ!";
    67	const P256_ORDER = BigInt(
    68	  "0xffffffff00000000ffffffffffffffffbce6faada7179e84f3b9cac2fc632551",
    69	);
    70	
    71	async function readUpstreamKey(name) {
    72	  const buf = await readFile(path.join(STAMPER_SNAPSHOT, name), "utf-8");
    73	  return buf.trim();
    74	}
    75	
    76	function decodeDerEcdsa(derHex) {
    77	  let i = 0;
    78	  const buf = Buffer.from(derHex, "hex");
    79	  if (buf[i++] !== 0x30) throw new Error("DER: not SEQUENCE");
    80	  let len = buf[i++];
    81	  if (len & 0x80) {
    82	    const n = len & 0x7f;
    83	    len = 0;
    84	    for (let k = 0; k < n; k++) len = (len << 8) | buf[i++];
    85	  }
    86	  if (buf[i++] !== 0x02) throw new Error("DER: r not INTEGER");
    87	  const rLen = buf[i++];
    88	  const r = buf.subarray(i, i + rLen);
    89	  i += rLen;
    90	  if (buf[i++] !== 0x02) throw new Error("DER: s not INTEGER");
    91	  const sLen = buf[i++];
    92	  const s = buf.subarray(i, i + sLen);
    93	  return {
    94	    r: BigInt("0x" + r.toString("hex")),
    95	    s: BigInt("0x" + s.toString("hex")),
    96	    rHex: r.toString("hex").replace(/^00+/, ""),
    97	    sHex: s.toString("hex").replace(/^00+/, ""),
    98	  };
    99	}
   100	
   101	function lowSEquivalent(sBig) {
   102	  return sBig > P256_ORDER / 2n ? P256_ORDER - sBig : sBig;
   103	}
   104	
   105	async function runPreflight() {
   106	  const stamper = new ApiKeyStamper({
   107	    apiPublicKey: PREFLIGHT_PUBLIC,
   108	    apiPrivateKey: PREFLIGHT_PRIVATE,
   109	    runtimeOverride: "purejs",
   110	  });
   111	  const decode = (s) =>
   112	    JSON.parse(Buffer.from(s.stampHeaderValue, "base64url").toString());
   113	
   114	  const stamp1 = await stamper.stamp(PREFLIGHT_MESSAGE);
   115	  const stamp2 = await stamper.stamp(PREFLIGHT_MESSAGE);
   116	  const j1 = decode(stamp1);
   117	  const j2 = decode(stamp2);
   118	
   119	  if (j1.signature !== j2.signature) {
   120	    throw new Error(
   121	      "preflight FAILED: purejs not deterministic. sig1=" +
   122	        j1.signature + " sig2=" + j2.signature,
   123	    );
   124	  }
   125	  if (j1.scheme !== "SIGNATURE_SCHEME_TK_API_P256") {
   126	    throw new Error("preflight FAILED: scheme " + j1.scheme);
   127	  }
   128	  if (j1.publicKey !== PREFLIGHT_PUBLIC) {
   129	    throw new Error("preflight FAILED: publicKey " + j1.publicKey);
   130	  }
   131	  const keys = Object.keys(j1);
   132	  if (
   133	    keys.length !== 3 ||
   134	    keys[0] !== "publicKey" ||
   135	    keys[1] !== "scheme" ||
   136	    keys[2] !== "signature"
   137	  ) {
   138	    throw new Error("preflight FAILED: key order " + keys.join(","));
   139	  }
   140	
   141	  // Verify the upstream signature against the upstream public key — both
   142	  // HIGH-S and LOW-S forms must verify, and r must match between them.
   143	  const sigDecoded = decodeDerEcdsa(j1.signature);
   144	  const hash = createHash("sha256").update(PREFLIGHT_MESSAGE).digest();
   145	  const verified = p256.verify(j1.signature, hash, PREFLIGHT_PUBLIC, {
   146	    lowS: false, // accept the upstream high-S form
   147	  });
   148	  if (!verified) {
   149	    throw new Error("preflight FAILED: upstream signature did not verify");
   150	  }
   151	
   152	  return {
   153	    privateKey: PREFLIGHT_PRIVATE,
   154	    publicKey: PREFLIGHT_PUBLIC,
   155	    message: PREFLIGHT_MESSAGE,
   156	    upstreamDerHex: j1.signature,
   157	    upstream_r: sigDecoded.rHex,
   158	    upstream_s: sigDecoded.sHex,
   159	    upstream_s_is_high_s: sigDecoded.s > P256_ORDER / 2n,
   160	    low_s_equivalent_s: lowSEquivalent(sigDecoded.s).toString(16),
   161	    note: "Upstream @noble/curves p256.sign defaults to HIGH-S in v1.x. " +
   162	      "C# port enforces LOW-S. The two signatures are cryptographically " +
   163	      "equivalent: same r, s' = n - s. C# tests assert r equality and " +
   164	      "verify the signature, not full DER byte equality.",
   165	    deterministic: true,
   166	    schemeOk: true,
   167	    keyOrderOk: true,
   168	  };
   169	}
   170	
   171	async function sha256OfFile(p) {
   172	  const buf = await readFile(p);
   173	  return createHash("sha256").update(buf).digest("hex");
   174	}
   175	function sha256OfString(s) {
   176	  return createHash("sha256").update(s, "utf-8").digest("hex");
   177	}
   178	async function generatorSelfSha256() {
   179	  return sha256OfFile(__filename);
   180	}
   181	async function transitiveLockSha256() {
   182	  const ls = execSync("npm ls --json --all", { cwd: __dirname, encoding: "utf-8" });
   183	  return createHash("sha256").update(ls).digest("hex");
   184	}
   185	
   186	async function main() {
   187	  const preflightResult = await runPreflight();
   188	  if (PREFLIGHT_ONLY) {
   189	    process.stdout.write(JSON.stringify(preflightResult, null, 2) + "\n");
   190	    return;
   191	  }
   192	
   193	  const privateKey = await readUpstreamKey("api-key.private");
   194	  const publicKey = await readUpstreamKey("api-key.public");
   195	  const messages = ["hello from TKHQ!", "another message", ""];
   196	
   197	  const stamper = new ApiKeyStamper({
   198	    apiPublicKey: publicKey,
   199	    apiPrivateKey: privateKey,
   200	    runtimeOverride: "purejs",
   201	  });
   202	
   203	  const stamps = [];
   204	  for (const m of messages) {
   205	    const stamp = await stamper.stamp(m);
   206	    const decoded = JSON.parse(
   207	      Buffer.from(stamp.stampHeaderValue, "base64url").toString(),
   208	    );
   209	    const sigDecoded = decodeDerEcdsa(decoded.signature);
   210	    stamps.push({
   211	      input: { message: m, privateKey, publicKey },
   212	      expected: {
   213	        stampHeaderName: stamp.stampHeaderName,
   214	        stampHeaderValueBase64Url: stamp.stampHeaderValue,
   215	        decoded,
   216	        // The pieces that C# can byte-compare regardless of low/high-S:
   217	        derived: {
   218	          r_hex: sigDecoded.rHex,
   219	          upstream_s_hex: sigDecoded.sHex,
   220	          upstream_s_is_high_s: sigDecoded.s > P256_ORDER / 2n,
   221	          low_s_equivalent_s_hex: lowSEquivalent(sigDecoded.s).toString(16),
   222	        },
   223	      },
   224	    });
   225	  }
   226	
   227	  const lockfilePath = path.join(__dirname, "package-lock.json");
   228	  const lockSha = await sha256OfFile(lockfilePath);
   229	  const genSha = await generatorSelfSha256();
   230	  const tLockSha = await transitiveLockSha256();
   231	
   232	  const dataBody = { preflight: preflightResult, stamps };
   233	  const outputSha = sha256OfString(JSON.stringify(dataBody));
   234	
   235	  const finalDoc = {
   236	    _provenance: {
   237	      level: "node-generated",
   238	      node_version: process.version,
   239	      npm_lockfile_sha256: lockSha,
   240	      generator_sha256: genSha,
   241	      transitive_lock_sha256: tLockSha,
   242	      output_sha256: outputSha,
   243	      upstream_pin: "@turnkey/api-key-stamper@0.5.0",
   244	      noble_curves_pin: "@noble/curves@1.3.0 (via npm overrides in package.json)",
   245	      generator_source: "tests/Fixtures/Generators/generate-stamper-vectors.mjs",
   246	      runtime_override: "purejs",
   247	      s_normalization: "upstream emits HIGH-S; fixture records both upstream_s and low_s_equivalent_s. C# port emits LOW-S; tests compare r equality and verify the signature.",
   248	    },
   249	    ...dataBody,
   250	  };
   251	
   252	  const outPath = path.join(
   253	    REPO_ROOT,
   254	    "tests",
   255	    "Fixtures",
   256	    "api-key-stamper",
   257	    "turnkey-stamper-node-vectors.json",
   258	  );
   259	  await writeFile(outPath, JSON.stringify(finalDoc, null, 2) + "\n", "utf-8");
   260	  process.stdout.write("Wrote " + outPath + "\n");
   261	}
   262	
   263	main().catch((err) => {
   264	  process.stderr.write(
   265	    "generate-stamper-vectors.mjs FAILED: " + (err.stack || err) + "\n",
   266	  );
   267	  process.exit(1);
   268	});

/bin/zsh -lc "nl -ba src/ApiKeyStamper.cs | sed -n '1,220p'" in /Users/takeshi/Kyuzan/src/turnkey-sdk-csharp/.claude/worktrees/laughing-hertz-048cd4
 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	// 1:1 logical port of @turnkey/api-key-stamper@0.5.0
     2	//
     3	// Upstream snapshot:
     4	//   codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/turnkey-api-key-stamper-0.5.0/
     5	//
     6	// Files covered:
     7	//   ts-source/index.ts                -> ApiKeyStamper class + signWithApiKey
     8	//                                         + stampHeaderName constant
     9	//   ts-source/purejs.ts               -> signWithApiKey "purejs" runtime
    10	//                                         (P-256 ECDSA via @noble/curves,
    11	//                                          SHA-256, DER hex output)
    12	//
    13	// Runtime selection note:
    14	//   The upstream package supports three runtimes — "browser" (WebCrypto),
    15	//   "node" (Node crypto), "purejs" (@noble/curves). This C# port mirrors
    16	//   the **purejs** runtime since BouncyCastle exposes the same primitives
    17	//   in a single backend. There is no runtime detection in C#; behavior is
    18	//   identical to what upstream produces when `runtimeOverride = "purejs"`
    19	//   is passed.
    20	//
    21	// Wire bytes:
    22	//   - signature.toDERHex() output equals upstream's noble signature.toDERHex().
    23	//   - The stamp JSON shape is exactly the upstream's
    24	//     { publicKey, scheme, signature } in this order.
    25	//   - The X-Stamp header value is base64url(JSON), matching upstream's
    26	//     `stringToBase64urlString(JSON.stringify(stamp))`.
    27	//   - SHA-256(content) and deterministic ECDSA (RFC 6979) are used; low-S is
    28	//     enforced (noble defaults to lowS: true).
    29	
    30	using System;
    31	using System.IO;
    32	using Org.BouncyCastle.Asn1.X9;
    33	using Org.BouncyCastle.Crypto.Parameters;
    34	using Org.BouncyCastle.Crypto.Signers;
    35	using Org.BouncyCastle.Math;
    36	using Org.BouncyCastle.Security;
    37	
    38	namespace Turnkey
    39	{
    40	    /// <summary>
    41	    /// Stamper for Turnkey API requests. 1:1 logical port of upstream
    42	    /// <c>@turnkey/api-key-stamper</c> at peak's pinned version 0.5.0.
    43	    /// </summary>
    44	    /// <remarks>
    45	    /// <para><b>Runtime parity target:</b> this port mirrors upstream's
    46	    /// <c>purejs</c> runtime (deterministic ECDSA via RFC 6979 + low-S).
    47	    /// Upstream's default <c>detectRuntime()</c> picks <c>"node"</c> in
    48	    /// Node which dispatches to <c>nodecrypto.ts</c> and produces
    49	    /// non-deterministic signatures (random k); behavior parity with
    50	    /// that runtime is intentionally NOT a goal — Turnkey's backend
    51	    /// accepts either, but the C# wire bytes will only match
    52	    /// deterministically against upstream <c>runtimeOverride: "purejs"</c>
    53	    /// callers. All three runtimes produce signatures that verify against
    54	    /// the same public key, so end-to-end Turnkey API calls work
    55	    /// regardless.</para>
    56	    /// <para><b>Validation timing:</b> the constructor parses but does NOT
    57	    /// validate the private key. Validation happens in
    58	    /// <see cref="SignWithApiKey(string)"/>, matching upstream which only
    59	    /// constructs noble's key object at sign time.</para>
    60	    /// </remarks>
    61	    public class ApiKeyStamper
    62	    {
    63	        /// <summary>Header name used by Turnkey API requests.</summary>
    64	        public const string StampHeaderName = "X-Stamp";
    65	
    66	        /// <summary>Turnkey signature scheme identifier for P-256 API keys.</summary>
    67	        public const string SignatureScheme = "SIGNATURE_SCHEME_TK_API_P256";
    68	
    69	        private readonly string _apiPublicKey;
    70	        private readonly string _apiPrivateKey;
    71	
    72	        /// <summary>
    73	        /// Initialize the stamper with a P-256 API key pair.
    74	        /// </summary>
    75	        /// <param name="apiPublicKey">Compressed P-256 public key as hex (66 chars).</param>
    76	        /// <param name="apiPrivateKey">P-256 private key scalar as 64 hex chars.</param>
    77	        /// <remarks>
    78	        /// The constructor only stores the strings. Key parsing and range
    79	        /// validation happen lazily in <see cref="SignWithApiKey(string)"/>,
    80	        /// matching upstream which builds noble's key object on each sign.
    81	        /// </remarks>
    82	        public ApiKeyStamper(string apiPublicKey, string apiPrivateKey)
    83	        {
    84	            // Upstream constructor only assigns config fields without
    85	            // validating; mirror that exactly. We do allow null here so a
    86	            // subsequent SignWithApiKey call surfaces the failure naturally.
    87	            _apiPublicKey = apiPublicKey!;
    88	            _apiPrivateKey = apiPrivateKey!;
    89	        }
    90	
    91	        /// <summary>
    92	        /// Output of <see cref="Stamp(string)"/>: the header name and the
    93	        /// base64url-encoded stamp JSON to use as the header value.
    94	        /// </summary>
    95	        public class StampResult
    96	        {
    97	            public string StampHeaderName { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    98	            public string StampHeaderValue { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    99	        }
   100	
   101	        /// <summary>
   102	        /// Internal JSON shape of the stamp. Field order matches upstream
   103	        /// (<c>publicKey, scheme, signature</c>) so the base64url-encoded
   104	        /// header value is wire-identical to what
   105	        /// <c>JSON.stringify({ publicKey, scheme, signature })</c> produces.
   106	        /// </summary>
   107	        public class TurnkeyStamp
   108	        {
   109	            [System.Text.Json.Serialization.JsonPropertyName("publicKey")]
   110	            public string PublicKey { get; set; } = string.Empty;
   111	
   112	            [System.Text.Json.Serialization.JsonPropertyName("scheme")]
   113	            public string Scheme { get; set; } = string.Empty;
   114	
   115	            [System.Text.Json.Serialization.JsonPropertyName("signature")]
   116	            public string Signature { get; set; } = string.Empty;
   117	        }
   118	
   119	        /// <summary>
   120	        /// Produce a Turnkey API stamp for <paramref name="payload"/>.
   121	        /// Equivalent to upstream <c>ApiKeyStamper.stamp(payload)</c>.
   122	        /// </summary>
   123	        public StampResult Stamp(string payload)
   124	        {
   125	            if (payload == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(payload));
   126	
   127	            string signatureDerHex = SignWithApiKey(payload);
   128	
   129	            var stamp = new TurnkeyStamp
   130	            {
   131	                PublicKey = _apiPublicKey,
   132	                Scheme = SignatureScheme,
   133	                Signature = signatureDerHex,
   134	            };
   135	
   136	            string stampJson = System.Text.Json.JsonSerializer.Serialize(
   137	                stamp, typeof(TurnkeyStamp), TurnkeyJsonContext.JsCompatibleOptions);
   138	
   139	            return new StampResult
   140	            {
   141	                StampHeaderName = StampHeaderName,
   142	                StampHeaderValue = Encoding.StringToBase64UrlString(stampJson),
   143	            };
   144	        }
   145	
   146	        /// <summary>
   147	        /// Mirror of upstream <c>purejs.ts signWithApiKey</c>. Verifies that
   148	        /// the configured public key matches the one derived from the
   149	        /// configured private key, then SHA-256-hashes the payload and signs
   150	        /// it with deterministic ECDSA (RFC 6979 + low-S) returning the
   151	        /// DER-encoded signature as a hex string.
   152	        /// </summary>
   153	        public string SignWithApiKey(string content)
   154	        {
   155	            if (content == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(content));
   156	
   157	            // Upstream `purejs.ts`:
   158	            //   const publicKey = p256.getPublicKey(input.privateKey, true);
   159	            //   const publicKeyString = uint8ArrayToHexString(publicKey);
   160	            //   if (publicKeyString != input.publicKey) throw new Error(...);
   161	            //
   162	            // Crypto.GetPublicKey enforces the noble invariants (exact 32-byte
   163	            // private key, scalar in [1, n - 1]) before deriving the public
   164	            // key. Per the upstream pattern this validation happens at sign
   165	            // time, not at constructor time.
   166	            byte[] derivedPublicKeyBytes = Crypto.GetPublicKey(_apiPrivateKey, isCompressed: true);
   167	            string derivedPublicKey = Encoding.Uint8ArrayToHexString(derivedPublicKeyBytes);
   168	            if (!string.Equals(derivedPublicKey, _apiPublicKey, StringComparison.Ordinal))
   169	            {
   170	                throw new InvalidOperationException(
   171	                    "Bad API key. Expected to get public key " + _apiPublicKey
   172	                    + ", got " + derivedPublicKey);
   173	            }
   174	
   175	            // Upstream:
   176	            //   const hash = createHash().update(input.content).digest();   // SHA-256
   177	            //   const signature = p256.sign(hash, input.privateKey);        // RFC 6979 + lowS
   178	            //   return signature.toDERHex();
   179	            var curve = ECNamedCurveTable.GetByName(CryptoConstants.CURVE_NAME);
   180	            var domainParams = new ECDomainParameters(curve.Curve, curve.G, curve.N, curve.H, curve.GetSeed());
   181	            var privateKeyBytes = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(_apiPrivateKey);
   182	            var privateKeyScalar = new BigInteger(1, privateKeyBytes);
   183	
   184	            byte[] payloadBytes = System.Text.Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(content);
   185	
   186	            var digest = DigestUtilities.GetDigest("SHA-256");
   187	            digest.BlockUpdate(payloadBytes, 0, payloadBytes.Length);
   188	            var hash = new byte[digest.GetDigestSize()];
   189	            digest.DoFinal(hash, 0);
   190	
   191	            var hmacCalculator = new HMacDsaKCalculator(DigestUtilities.GetDigest("SHA-256"));
   192	            var signer = new ECDsaSigner(hmacCalculator);
   193	            signer.Init(true, new ECPrivateKeyParameters(privateKeyScalar, domainParams));
   194	
   195	            BigInteger[] signature = signer.GenerateSignature(hash);
   196	            BigInteger r = signature[0];
   197	            BigInteger s = signature[1];
   198	
   199	            // Low-S normalization. @turnkey/api-key-stamper@0.5.0 depends on
   200	            // @noble/curves@^1.3.0, and noble v1.3.0
   201	            // (src/abstract/weierstrass.ts) defaults to lowS=true:
   202	            //   let { lowS, prehash, extraEntropy: ent } = opts;
   203	            //   if (lowS == null) lowS = true; // RFC6979 3.2
   204	            // The upstream purejs.ts call `p256.sign(hash, privateKey)` passes
   205	            // no opts, so the runtime emits low-S signatures. We reproduce
   206	            // that here by clamping s into (0, n/2].
   207	            BigInteger halfN = domainParams.N.ShiftRight(1);
   208	            if (s.CompareTo(halfN) > 0)
   209	            {
   210	                s = domainParams.N.Subtract(s);
   211	            }
   212	
   213	            return EncodeDerSignatureHex(r, s);
   214	        }
   215	
   216	        /// <summary>
   217	        /// Encode the <c>(r, s)</c> pair as a DER ASN.1 SEQUENCE of two
   218	        /// INTEGERs, then hex-encode the result.
   219	        /// Equivalent to noble's <c>signature.toDERHex()</c>.
   220	        /// </summary>

    68	        #region Constants
    69	
    70	        /// <summary>
    71	        /// Constants from upstream <c>constants.ts</c> used by this port.

/bin/zsh -lc "nl -ba tests/ProofFixtureProvenanceTests.cs | sed -n '1,280p'" in /Users/takeshi/Kyuzan/src/turnkey-sdk-csharp/.claude/worktrees/laughing-hertz-048cd4
 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	// ProofFixtureProvenanceTests.cs — PR-11
     2	//
     3	// Asserts the structural integrity and provenance of the upstream proof
     4	// fixture JSON committed at tests/Fixtures/proofs/. The C# proof
     5	// verifier is OUT OF SCOPE per plan Section 12; this test class
     6	// guarantees only:
     7	//
     8	//   1. The fixture JSON parses.
     9	//   2. _provenance carries the expected schema (level, upstream_file,
    10	//      upstream_file_sha256, upstream_package, upstream_package_version).
    11	//   3. The sha256 recorded in _provenance matches the actual sha256 of
    12	//      the cited upstream snapshot file (detects manual edits to either
    13	//      the fixture or the upstream snapshot tree).
    14	//   4. Each appProofs entry has the v1AppProof fields
    15	//      (scheme, publicKey, proofPayload, signature) populated with
    16	//      plausible types (P-256 ephemeral key hex length 264, DER-ish
    17	//      hex strings, SIGNATURE_SCHEME_EPHEMERAL_KEY_P256).
    18	//   5. Each bootProofs entry has the v1BootProof fields populated:
    19	//      ephemeralPublicKeyHex, awsAttestationDocB64, qosManifestB64,
    20	//      qosManifestEnvelopeB64, deploymentLabel, enclaveApp, owner,
    21	//      createdAt {seconds, nanos}.
    22	
    23	using System;
    24	using System.IO;
    25	using System.Linq;
    26	using System.Security.Cryptography;
    27	using System.Text.Json;
    28	using FluentAssertions;
    29	using Xunit;
    30	
    31	namespace Turnkey.Tests
    32	{
    33	    public class ProofFixtureProvenanceTests
    34	    {
    35	        private static readonly string FixturePath = Path.Combine(
    36	            AppContext.BaseDirectory,
    37	            "Fixtures",
    38	            "proofs",
    39	            "upstream-proof-tests-fixture.json");
    40	
    41	        // The fixture is shipped under tests/Fixtures/proofs/ at repo root.
    42	        // AppContext.BaseDirectory points at .../tests/bin/Release/net8.0/.
    43	        // The upstream snapshot it cites lives outside the test bin dir;
    44	        // we resolve the snapshot path by walking up to the repo root.
    45	        private static string ResolveRepoRoot()
    46	        {
    47	            // tests/bin/Release/net8.0/  -> walk up to ".claude/worktrees/<x>"
    48	            // or the actual repo root (containing turnkey-sdk-csharp.sln).
    49	            string dir = AppContext.BaseDirectory;
    50	            for (int i = 0; i < 8; i++)
    51	            {
    52	                if (File.Exists(Path.Combine(dir, "turnkey-sdk-csharp.sln")))
    53	                {
    54	                    return dir;
    55	                }
    56	                dir = Path.GetDirectoryName(dir)!;
    57	            }
    58	            throw new InvalidOperationException(
    59	                "could not locate repo root from " + AppContext.BaseDirectory);
    60	        }
    61	
    62	        [Fact]
    63	        public void FixtureFile_Exists_AndParsesAsJson()
    64	        {
    65	            File.Exists(FixturePath).Should().BeTrue(
    66	                $"fixture must be committed at {FixturePath}");
    67	
    68	            using var doc = JsonDocument.Parse(File.ReadAllText(FixturePath));
    69	            doc.RootElement.ValueKind.Should().Be(JsonValueKind.Object);
    70	        }
    71	
    72	        [Fact]
    73	        public void Provenance_SchemaIsComplete()
    74	        {
    75	            using var doc = JsonDocument.Parse(File.ReadAllText(FixturePath));
    76	            var prov = doc.RootElement.GetProperty("_provenance");
    77	
    78	            prov.GetProperty("level").GetString().Should().Be("upstream-test-vectors");
    79	            prov.GetProperty("upstream_file").GetString().Should().StartWith(
    80	                "codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/turnkey-crypto-");
    81	            prov.GetProperty("upstream_file_sha256").GetString().Should().MatchRegex("^[0-9a-f]{64}$");
    82	            prov.GetProperty("upstream_package").GetString().Should().Be("@turnkey/crypto");
    83	            prov.GetProperty("upstream_package_version").GetString().Should().NotBeNullOrWhiteSpace();
    84	        }
    85	
    86	        [Fact]
    87	        public void Provenance_UpstreamFileSha256_MatchesActualSnapshotBytes()
    88	        {
    89	            using var doc = JsonDocument.Parse(File.ReadAllText(FixturePath));
    90	            var prov = doc.RootElement.GetProperty("_provenance");
    91	            string upstreamRel = prov.GetProperty("upstream_file").GetString()!;
    92	            string recordedSha = prov.GetProperty("upstream_file_sha256").GetString()!;
    93	
    94	            string repoRoot = ResolveRepoRoot();
    95	            string upstreamAbs = Path.Combine(repoRoot, upstreamRel);
    96	
    97	            File.Exists(upstreamAbs).Should().BeTrue(
    98	                $"upstream snapshot file cited in provenance must exist: {upstreamAbs}");
    99	
   100	            byte[] bytes = File.ReadAllBytes(upstreamAbs);
   101	            string actualSha = Convert.ToHexString(SHA256.HashData(bytes)).ToLowerInvariant();
   102	
   103	            actualSha.Should().Be(
   104	                recordedSha,
   105	                "fixture provenance sha256 must match the actual bytes of the cited upstream snapshot file. " +
   106	                "If this fails, either the fixture is stale or the upstream snapshot was edited locally.");
   107	        }
   108	
   109	        [Fact]
   110	        public void AppProofs_StructuralSchema_IsCorrect()
   111	        {
   112	            using var doc = JsonDocument.Parse(File.ReadAllText(FixturePath));
   113	            var arr = doc.RootElement.GetProperty("appProofs");
   114	            arr.GetArrayLength().Should().BeGreaterThan(0);
   115	
   116	            foreach (var entry in arr.EnumerateArray())
   117	            {
   118	                entry.GetProperty("scheme").GetString().Should().Be(
   119	                    "SIGNATURE_SCHEME_EPHEMERAL_KEY_P256");
   120	
   121	                string publicKey = entry.GetProperty("publicKey").GetString()!;
   122	                publicKey.Should().MatchRegex("^[0-9a-fA-F]+$");
   123	                // The upstream ephemeralPublicKey form is 2 P-256 uncompressed
   124	                // points concatenated (65 + 65 = 130 bytes => 260 hex chars,
   125	                // or with prefix 04 already present => same).
   126	                publicKey.Length.Should().BeInRange(130, 264,
   127	                    "expected P-256 uncompressed-pair hex (130 chars) or longer");
   128	
   129	                string proofPayload = entry.GetProperty("proofPayload").GetString()!;
   130	                proofPayload.Should().StartWith("{").And.EndWith("}");
   131	                // Parse the nested JSON.
   132	                using var payloadDoc = JsonDocument.Parse(proofPayload);
   133	                payloadDoc.RootElement.GetProperty("type").GetString()
   134	                    .Should().Be("APP_PROOF_TYPE_ADDRESS_DERIVATION");
   135	
   136	                string signature = entry.GetProperty("signature").GetString()!;
   137	                signature.Should().MatchRegex("^[0-9a-fA-F]+$");
   138	                signature.Length.Should().BeInRange(64, 256,
   139	                    "P-256 signature in compact-bytes hex (64 chars min) or DER hex");
   140	            }
   141	        }
   142	
   143	        [Fact]
   144	        public void BootProofs_StructuralSchema_IsCorrect()
   145	        {
   146	            using var doc = JsonDocument.Parse(File.ReadAllText(FixturePath));
   147	            var arr = doc.RootElement.GetProperty("bootProofs");
   148	            arr.GetArrayLength().Should().BeGreaterThan(0);
   149	
   150	            foreach (var entry in arr.EnumerateArray())
   151	            {
   152	                string ephHex = entry.GetProperty("ephemeralPublicKeyHex").GetString()!;
   153	                ephHex.Should().MatchRegex("^[0-9a-fA-F]+$");
   154	
   155	                // AWS attestation + QOS manifests are base64.
   156	                string awsB64 = entry.GetProperty("awsAttestationDocB64").GetString()!;
   157	                Action act = () => Convert.FromBase64String(awsB64);
   158	                act.Should().NotThrow(
   159	                    "awsAttestationDocB64 must be valid base64");
   160	
   161	                string qmB64 = entry.GetProperty("qosManifestB64").GetString()!;
   162	                Action act2 = () => Convert.FromBase64String(qmB64);
   163	                act2.Should().NotThrow("qosManifestB64 must be valid base64");
   164	
   165	                string qmEnvB64 = entry.GetProperty("qosManifestEnvelopeB64").GetString()!;
   166	                Action act3 = () => Convert.FromBase64String(qmEnvB64);
   167	                act3.Should().NotThrow("qosManifestEnvelopeB64 must be valid base64");
   168	
   169	                entry.GetProperty("deploymentLabel").GetString()
   170	                    .Should().NotBeNullOrWhiteSpace();
   171	                entry.GetProperty("enclaveApp").GetString()
   172	                    .Should().Be("signer");
   173	                entry.GetProperty("owner").GetString()
   174	                    .Should().Be("tkhq");
   175	
   176	                var createdAt = entry.GetProperty("createdAt");
   177	                createdAt.GetProperty("seconds").GetString()
   178	                    .Should().MatchRegex("^[0-9]+$");
   179	                createdAt.GetProperty("nanos").GetString()
   180	                    .Should().MatchRegex("^[0-9]+$");
   181	            }
   182	        }
   183	
   184	        [Fact]
   185	        public void AppProofs_And_BootProofs_HaveMatchingPublicKeys()
   186	        {
   187	            // The upstream test pairs (appProof_i, bootProof_i) so that
   188	            // appProof.publicKey == bootProof.ephemeralPublicKeyHex.
   189	            using var doc = JsonDocument.Parse(File.ReadAllText(FixturePath));
   190	            var apps = doc.RootElement.GetProperty("appProofs").EnumerateArray().ToList();
   191	            var boots = doc.RootElement.GetProperty("bootProofs").EnumerateArray().ToList();
   192	
   193	            apps.Count.Should().Be(boots.Count,
   194	                "appProofs and bootProofs arrays must be paired (same length)");
   195	
   196	            for (int i = 0; i < apps.Count; i++)
   197	            {
   198	                apps[i].GetProperty("publicKey").GetString()
   199	                    .Should().Be(
   200	                        boots[i].GetProperty("ephemeralPublicKeyHex").GetString(),
   201	                        $"appProof[{i}].publicKey must equal bootProof[{i}].ephemeralPublicKeyHex (upstream pairing rule)");
   202	            }
   203	        }
   204	    }
   205	}

    63	  test("should verify valid app proof signatures", () => {
    64	    expect(verifyAppProofSignature(testAppProof1)).toBeUndefined();
    65	    expect(verifyAppProofSignature(testAppProof2)).toBeUndefined();
    66	  });
    67	
    68	  test("should verify correct app proof / boot proof combos", async () => {
    69	    await expect(
    70	      verify(testAppProof1, testBootProof1),
    71	    ).resolves.toBeUndefined();
    72	    await expect(
    73	      verify(testAppProof2, testBootProof2),
    74	    ).resolves.toBeUndefined();
    75	  });
    76	
    77	  test("should NOT verify with malformed app proofs", () => {
    78	    let malformedAppProof2 = { ...testAppProof2 };
    79	
    80	    // Wrong publicKey - should cause signature verification failure
    81	    malformedAppProof2.publicKey = testAppProof1.publicKey;
    82	    expect(() => verifyAppProofSignature(malformedAppProof2)).toThrow(
    83	      "Signature verification failed",
    84	    );
    85	    malformedAppProof2.publicKey = testAppProof2.publicKey;
    86	
    87	    // Wrong proofPayload - should cause signature verification failure
    88	    malformedAppProof2.proofPayload = testAppProof1.proofPayload;
    89	    expect(() => verifyAppProofSignature(malformedAppProof2)).toThrow(
    90	      "Signature verification failed",
    91	    );
    92	    malformedAppProof2.proofPayload = testAppProof2.proofPayload;
    93	
    94	    // Wrong signature - should cause signature verification failure
    95	    malformedAppProof2.signature = testAppProof1.signature;
    96	    expect(() => verifyAppProofSignature(malformedAppProof2)).toThrow(
    97	      "Signature verification failed",
    98	    );
    99	  });
   100	
   101	  test("should NOT verify with malformed boot proofs", async () => {
   102	    let malformedBootProof2 = { ...testBootProof2 };
   103	
   104	    // Wrong ephemeral key - should cause ephemeral key mismatch
   105	    malformedBootProof2.ephemeralPublicKeyHex =
   106	      testBootProof1.ephemeralPublicKeyHex;
   107	    await expect(verify(testAppProof2, malformedBootProof2)).rejects.toThrow(
   108	      "Ephemeral pub keys from app proof:",
   109	    );
   110	    malformedBootProof2.ephemeralPublicKeyHex =
   111	      testBootProof2.ephemeralPublicKeyHex;
   112	
   113	    // Wrong awsAttestationDocB64 - causes ephemeral key mistmatch error because the boot proofs have the same qos manifest, so the user data check doesn't fail
   114	    malformedBootProof2.awsAttestationDocB64 =
   115	      testBootProof1.awsAttestationDocB64;
   116	    await expect(verify(testAppProof2, malformedBootProof2)).rejects.toThrow(
   117	      "Ephemeral pub keys from app proof:",
   118	    );
   119	    malformedBootProof2.awsAttestationDocB64 =
   120	      testBootProof2.awsAttestationDocB64;
   121	
   122	    // Wrong qosManifestB64 (randomly generated) - should cause user_data verification failure
   123	    malformedBootProof2.qosManifestB64 =
   124	      "puwpDDoA3dqZpFV0nDnSgj2iFyy2VDUnDSE7u+awts0=";
   125	    await expect(verify(testAppProof2, malformedBootProof2)).rejects.toThrow(
   126	      "attestationDoc's user_data doesn't match the hash of the manifest. ",
   127	    );
   128	  });
   129	});

/bin/zsh -lc "nl -ba tests/Fixtures/Generators/README.md | sed -n '1,160p'" in /Users/takeshi/Kyuzan/src/turnkey-sdk-csharp/.claude/worktrees/laughing-hertz-048cd4
 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	# Tests/Fixtures/Generators — Node-side fixture generators
     2	
     3	The scripts in this directory consume the **pinned upstream npm packages**
     4	and emit byte-snapshot JSON files under `tests/Fixtures/{http,api-key-stamper,crypto}/`.
     5	The C# test suite reads those JSON files and asserts byte-equal outputs
     6	for the deterministic paths (stamper PureJS, credential-bundle decrypt,
     7	export-bundle decrypt, signed-request body).
     8	
     9	This directory is **excluded from `dotnet build`** via the
    10	`<Content Remove="Fixtures/Generators/**"/>` lines in
    11	`tests/turnkey-sdk-csharp.Tests.csproj`. Node is therefore **not a
    12	prerequisite for `dotnet test`** in normal CI — the committed JSON
    13	fixtures are the source of truth.
    14	
    15	## Pinned versions
    16	
    17	| Package | Version | Source |
    18	|---|---|---|
    19	| `@turnkey/crypto` | 2.8.8 | matches `codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/turnkey-crypto-2.8.8/` |
    20	| `@turnkey/http` | 3.16.0 | matches `codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/turnkey-http-3.16.0/` |
    21	| `@turnkey/api-key-stamper` | 0.5.0 | matches `codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/turnkey-api-key-stamper-0.5.0/` |
    22	| `@turnkey/encoding` | 0.6.0 | matches `codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/turnkey-encoding-0.6.0/` |
    23	
    24	The transitive `@noble/curves` resolution in `package-lock.json` decides
    25	whether `signWithApiKey({ runtimeOverride: "purejs" })` produces RFC 6979
    26	deterministic-k low-S signatures. The generator scripts MUST run a
    27	pre-flight assertion against a known hex vector and exit non-zero if the
    28	resolved noble version diverges from RFC 6979.
    29	
    30	## Reproduction
    31	
    32	Requires Node ≥ 20.10. The plan target is **Node 20.x**, but anything in
    33	the supported range that ships an unchanged `@noble/curves` is
    34	acceptable — the generator's pre-flight pre-flight assertion is the
    35	final gate.
    36	
    37	```bash
    38	# From the repo root
    39	cd tests/Fixtures/Generators
    40	npm ci          # restore exact pinned versions from package-lock.json
    41	npm run gen:all # regenerate all JSON fixtures
    42	```
    43	
    44	The resulting JSON files include a `_provenance` object recording:
    45	
    46	- `level` (always `"node-generated"`)
    47	- `node_version` (`process.version`)
    48	- `npm_lockfile_sha256` (sha256 of this directory's `package-lock.json`)
    49	- `generator_sha256` (sha256 of the `.mjs` script that produced the file)
    50	- `transitive_lock_sha256` (sha256 of `npm ls --json` output, used to
    51	  detect drift in `@noble/curves` resolution)
    52	- `output_sha256` (self-hash of the data section, excluding the
    53	  provenance object itself)
    54	
    55	## CI integration
    56	
    57	The committed JSON fixtures are byte-compared in `dotnet test`. Node is
    58	**never invoked** by the main CI workflow (`.github/workflows/ci.yml`)
    59	nor the release workflow. A separate opt-in workflow
    60	`.github/workflows/fixture-regen.yml` (added in PR-13) re-runs these
    61	generators on demand and opens a PR if the output diverges.
    62	
    63	## Why pure shell + Node, no TypeScript
    64	
    65	These scripts are intentionally `.mjs` (native ESM) with **no
    66	TypeScript build step**. The fewer build tools sit between this directory
    67	and the pinned upstream packages, the fewer chances for transitive
    68	resolution drift. Each script is a single file ≤ ~150 lines.
    69	
    70	## Out of scope
    71	
    72	- This directory does NOT contain `proof.ts` golden fixtures —
    73	  those live under `tests/Fixtures/proofs/` and were copied directly
    74	  from upstream `__tests__/proof-tests.ts` (no execution path needed,
    75	  the proof verifier itself is unported per plan Section 12).
    76	- This directory does NOT generate QOS encryption vectors —
    77	  `quorumKeyEncrypt` is out of plan scope (see Section 2.1).

     1	# Turnkey upstream source pins
     2	
     3	The C# port targets the **peak-pinned** Turnkey npm versions, NOT the Unity
     4	port's newer versions. The npm tarball contents (extracted under
     5	[`upstream-snapshots/`](./upstream-snapshots/)) are the authoritative source.
     6	GitHub SHAs are secondary metadata.
     7	
     8	## Pin table
     9	
    10	| src C# file                | Upstream snapshot path                  | npm package                | Version | Tarball sha256 |
    11	|---|---|---|---|---|
    12	| src/Encoding.cs            | turnkey-encoding-0.6.0                  | @turnkey/encoding          | 0.6.0   | `2cf9e6ee1f47ac7e3cc3e644cdb0e3e112c906a6ea1af737777f4658b73fb7bc` |
    13	| src/CryptoConstants.cs     | turnkey-crypto-2.8.8                    | @turnkey/crypto            | 2.8.8   | `75115706fccc29c664f9f918d9a0c2c1798eb03f261cb5b0c186c75663cf79d3` |
    14	| src/Crypto.cs              | turnkey-crypto-2.8.8                    | @turnkey/crypto            | 2.8.8   | `75115706fccc29c664f9f918d9a0c2c1798eb03f261cb5b0c186c75663cf79d3` |
    15	| src/ApiKeyStamper.cs       | turnkey-api-key-stamper-0.5.0           | @turnkey/api-key-stamper   | 0.5.0   | `962a2d22c7c40240f05be98533769b37ab7dad7dbb5abec762c41007233d02bd` |
    16	| src/Http.cs                | turnkey-http-3.16.0                     | @turnkey/http              | 3.16.0  | `d849f2156633f63062c52067785df1ce33eac0659044df932862c5d6de9dbdaf` |
    17	| src/TurnkeyJsonContext.cs  | turnkey-crypto-2.8.8                    | (no single upstream; covers DTOs from crypto + api-key-stamper + http) | n/a | n/a |
    18	
    19	Each upstream snapshot directory contains:
    20	
    21	- `package/` — verbatim npm tarball extract (the authoritative wire-format
    22	  source: `dist/*.js` + `dist/*.d.ts` + `package.json` + LICENSE / README).
    23	- `ts-source/` — the original TypeScript source from `github.com/tkhq/sdk` at
    24	  the matching git tag SHA (committed for human readability; the npm tarball
    25	  remains the wire-format source of truth if the two ever disagree).
    26	
    27	## Why these versions
    28	
    29	These are exactly what the peak monorepo pulls. See
    30	[`peak-lockfile-evidence.md`](./peak-lockfile-evidence.md) for the
    31	`pnpm-lock.yaml` lines.
    32	
    33	## GitHub commit SHAs (secondary)
    34	
    35	`gitHead` is **NOT present** in the published tarballs for these versions
    36	(`grep gitHead package/package.json` returns nothing for any of the four).
    37	The GitHub commit SHAs below are resolved from the git tag of the form
    38	`@turnkey/<pkg>@<version>` via `gh api /repos/tkhq/sdk/git/ref/tags/...`.
    39	These are recorded for cross-reference only. The npm tarball sha256 above
    40	is the controlling wire-format source.
    41	
    42	| npm package                | Version | Git tag SHA                                  | Reference URL |
    43	|---|---|---|---|
    44	| @turnkey/encoding          | 0.6.0   | `60a997f4c52ac5f98bdd285af934f02699b88bff`   | https://github.com/tkhq/sdk/tree/60a997f4c52ac5f98bdd285af934f02699b88bff/packages/encoding |
    45	| @turnkey/crypto            | 2.8.8   | `b35dc642bd7c1728f97acd43d4cba66976b65084`   | https://github.com/tkhq/sdk/tree/b35dc642bd7c1728f97acd43d4cba66976b65084/packages/crypto |
    46	| @turnkey/api-key-stamper   | 0.5.0   | `b711befbb88ec522452dbdac68f0e98762be10dd`   | https://github.com/tkhq/sdk/tree/b711befbb88ec522452dbdac68f0e98762be10dd/packages/api-key-stamper |
    47	| @turnkey/http              | 3.16.0  | `8def9ba521233137437ac7294693a4ae0a0d14da`   | https://github.com/tkhq/sdk/tree/8def9ba521233137437ac7294693a4ae0a0d14da/packages/http |
    48	
    49	## Re-pinning procedure
    50	
    51	When bumping any pin:
    52	
    53	1. Update the table above (npm version, refresh tarball sha256, gitHead).
    54	2. Update `Directory.Packages.props` or any version comment.
    55	3. Re-run `npm pack` and refresh the extracted directories under
    56	   `upstream-snapshots/`.
    57	4. Re-run **3 Codex review rounds per affected file** via
    58	   [`codex-crypto-review.sh`](./codex-crypto-review.sh).
    59	5. Update `CHANGELOG.md`.

**A. Diff Overview**

Intent acknowledged: this PR ships the machine-verifiable equivalence-test infrastructure around the C# SDK and pinned upstream Turnkey TypeScript packages, implementing parts of `plans/PLAN-EQUIVALENCE-VERIFICATION.md`.

Commits reviewed:
- `a0fd24d` docs: add equivalence verification plan v3
- `ef3ed59` docs(PR-1b): peak usage evidence for unported APIs
- `1a1529e` test(PR-2): upstream-to-C# coverage matrix scaffolding
- `76de11e` test(PR-3): DecryptExportBundle vectors + coverage gate
- `2519b2c` test(PR-4): Node fixture generator scaffolding
- `2a8df82` test(PR-6): Node-generated stamper vectors
- `c959e2a` ci(PR-12): upstream drift workflow
- `ccce1ed` test(PR-11): proof fixture provenance tests
- `d7871bc` docs(PR-14): README posture + NOTICE attributions

Implemented: PR-1, PR-1b, PR-2, PR-3, PR-4, PR-6, PR-11, PR-12, PR-14.  
Explicitly deferred per plan table: PR-5, PR-7, PR-7a, PR-8, PR-9, PR-9b, PR-10, PR-13/PR-13b.

**B. Cryptographic Correctness Audit**

No security or cryptographic correctness defect found.

PR-6 stamper fixture math is correct. I checked the P-256 order relation for all fixture entries and preflight: each upstream `s` is high-S, each recorded low-S value satisfies `s_low = n - s_high`, and `s_low <= n/2`. The C# test also verifies both upstream high-S and C# low-S signatures against the same public key and asserts `r` equality in `tests/ApiKeyStamperTests.cs:284-296`.

PR-3 `enclaveQuorumPublic` matches `Crypto.Constants.PRODUCTION_SIGNER_SIGN_PUBLIC_KEY` byte-for-byte:
- upstream bundle: `codex-crypto-reviews/.../crypto-test.ts:115`
- C# constant: `src/Crypto.cs:114-115`
- embedded C# test bundle: `tests/CryptoTests.cs:633-639`

PR-11 proof fixture schema matches upstream JSON:
- app proof scheme is `SIGNATURE_SCHEME_EPHEMERAL_KEY_P256`
- boot proof has `enclaveApp=signer`, `owner=tkhq`
- paired `appProof.publicKey == bootProof.ephemeralPublicKeyHex`
Covered by `tests/ProofFixtureProvenanceTests.cs:118-134`, `:169-180`, and `:184-202`.

**C. CI / Operational Risk**

No unbounded operational risk found.

Coverage gate in `.github/workflows/ci.yml:50-51` runs `coverage-map.sh --check`. The script depends on `bash`, `find`, `sort`, `awk`, `mktemp`, and normal file writes in the checkout. It does not call `gh`, Node, npm, or dotnet.

Upstream drift workflow permissions look sufficient for a private current repo: `contents: read` supports checkout; `issues: write` covers `gh label create`, `gh issue list/edit/comment/create/close`; `gh api` reads public `tkhq/sdk` contents at pinned SHAs. See `.github/workflows/upstream-drift.yml:28-31`, `:114`, and `:161-203`.

`package-lock.json` has no `os`/`cpu` platform restrictions. The only “optional” item I found is the optional `encoding` peer for `node-fetch`, not a platform-specific install path.

**D. Plan-Consistency Audit**

Finding D1: README still overstates the current Tier-2 enforcement surface.

The README says equivalence is enforced by four mechanisms and describes Tier-2 as bytes from pinned upstream npm packages, but the only committed Tier-2 C# assertion listed is the stamper fixture test. Deferred plan items still include HTTP byte vectors, HPKE round-trip/structural fixtures, HPKE/RFC9180 evaluation, standard vectors, NIST vectors, cross-language constants, and fixture regeneration workflow (`plans/PLAN-EQUIVALENCE-VERIFICATION.md:582-594`). The README does disclose Tier-3 partial HKDF-only coverage (`README.md:91`) and HPKE/RFC uncertainty (`README.md:132-136`), but it does not explicitly say PR-5 HTTP byte equality and PR-7 HPKE Node-generated fixtures are not yet enforced.

Relevant lines:
- `README.md:83-91`
- `README.md:132-136`
- `plans/PLAN-EQUIVALENCE-VERIFICATION.md:582-594`

Coverage map status: no `MISSING` rows in `coverage-map.tsv`; only the markdown legend contains the word `MISSING`.

**E. C# / Test Code Quality**

No blocking test-code quality issue found.

`ApiKeyStamperTests.NodeFixture_StamperByteParity_PureJsRfc6979` uses `GetProperty`, which fails with explicit JSON/property exceptions on malformed fixtures rather than `NullReferenceException`. Nullable `GetString()!` values flow into APIs that throw argument/format failures on invalid inputs.

`ResolveRepoRoot` walking 8 directories is enough for the normal GitHub Actions test output layout (`repo/tests/bin/Release/net8.0` resolves in about 4 ascents). No blocking magic-number/string issue found; the protocol literals are intentionally asserted as wire-format constants.

**F. Documentation / Attribution**

No attribution defect found.

NOTICE points Apache-2.0 upstream borrowings back to `tkhq/sdk` and `turnkey-source-pins.md`, which records git tag SHAs and repo URLs (`NOTICE:31-39`, `codex-crypto-reviews/turnkey-source-pins.md:42-47`). The proof fixture also carries upstream file path and SHA provenance in `tests/Fixtures/proofs/upstream-proof-tests-fixture.json:2-8`.

README is clear that stamper “byte-equal” is not full DER equality because upstream high-S and C# low-S differ; it defines the equivalence as same `r`, `s_low = n - s_high`, and both signatures verifying (`README.md:124-131`).

**G. Unresolved / Not Verified**

I could not run `dotnet test` or `coverage-map.sh --check` in this round because the sandbox is read-only and those checks write build/output or regenerated report files. Static inspection found one documentation consistency finding: D1 above.
